# ROADMAP ŌĆö Living Frontier Ledger
> The persistent, dynamic task ledger for an exploratory project. Survives across sessions (unlike a session's scratch task list). Update it at the end of every session: move items between **Inbox / Now / Open / Parked / Done**. This is where "what were we doing?" gets answered without re-deriving it.

## Inbox ŌĆö capture diversions here, DON'T chase them
> The rule (Chris's): when something shiny appears mid-session, it gets a ticket here ŌĆö it does **not** hijack the current focus. "Ooh, something new!" ŌåÆ write it down, keep going. Triage Inbox ŌåÆ Open/Parked at session end. A diversion captured is free; a diversion chased costs the thread.

- ~~**Ō¢Č­¤ö┤ FOUNDATIONAL DECOMPILER BUG ŌĆö compare opcodes render INVERTED direction**~~ **FIXED 2026-06-04 (ORACLE-CONFIRMED, commit pending).** `vm_decompile.py`'s hand-written opcodeŌåÆmnemonic map had **FOUR** compares wrong (the oracle sweep found one more than the first triage): the regular layout is signed `[lt,le,gt,ge]`=C2-C5, unsigned `[lt,le,gt,ge]`=C6-C9, but the map had **C3/C5 leŌåöge swapped** (`sge`/`sle` ŌåÆ should be `sle`/`sge`) AND **C6/C9 ltŌåöge swapped** (`uge`/`ult` ŌåÆ should be `ult`/`uge`). Each verified vs the live ROM handler (`step_one_vm_op`, regL/regR matrix incl. ŌłÆ1-vs-1 for signedness); the **opcode table `vm-opcodes-v2.toml` was RIGHT all along** (SCMP*/UCMP*) ŌĆö only the decompiler's map drifted. **Blast radius: 323 comparison sites flipped** across all 4 banks (e.g. `seek_enemyŌĆ”` `} while (local11 >= 6)` ŌåÆ the correct `< 6`; `if (rng_mod(100) >= threshold)` ŌåÆ `< threshold`). It survived because the **arithmetic** formulas are oracle-verified but comparison-DIRECTION in control flow was never exercised ŌĆö the exact [[feedback_foundation_discipline_early]] trap. **The gates structurally can't catch it** (round-trip = bytecode untouched; CFG-gate orientation flips consistently on raw+structured) ŌåÆ built **`tools/probe-compare-opcodes.py`** as the permanent primitive-layer validator (oracle truth table vs decompiler map + `_BINOP` + toml; exit 1 on drift). All gates stay green post-fix (cfg 495/495, round-trip CLEAN, drift CLEAN, --check 0 BAD, test-vm-cfg 74). **LESSON (Chris): the VM is more robust than it first appears ŌĆö keep oracle-verifying primitives; structural gates pass over semantic-direction bugs.** [[feedback_foundation_discipline_early]] [[feedback_silent_tool_failure_hallucination]]
- ~~**Ō¢Č DECOMPILER BUG ŌĆö value-producing conditional (ternary) renders as empty `if(){}else{}` and DROPS a value**~~ **FIXED (forward cases) 2026-06-04 ŌĆö and the same trap as the compare bug: gate-invisible, oracle-validated.** A value-diamond (`regA = cond ? a : b` ŌĆö two value-loading arms converging) was rendered as empty `if(){}else{}` / gotos-to-empty-labels with only ONE arm's value surviving (e.g. `spawn_zealot(...)(1)` instead of `(flag ? 0 : 1)`; `min_word`/`max_word` returned a single hardcoded arg). **Confirmed a 2nd surface form Chris found (`$A7DC`): the empty-`if/else` scan (72) UNDER-counted ŌĆö a bytecode scan for the converging value-diamond shape found 80 sites / 65 subs, incl. 24 feeding `return` (functions returning the wrong value) + 22 call-args + stores.** **FIX = coordinated expression-engine + CFG-gate change:** (1) `vm_cfg.value_diamonds` detects the shape (forward layout `head<fall<taken<merge`, each arm sole-pred = head, call-free cond); the decode loop folds it to `(cond ? vt : vf)` (`_ternary_expr`; polarity from branch_z/nz + which arm is fall vs taken), suppressing the head branch + fall jump + now-dead labels. (2) `vm_cfg.bytecode_cfg` CONTRACTS the same diamonds into their merge (a value-diamond is an EXPRESSION, not control flow ŌĆö like C `?:`) so `lower(raw)==bytecode_cfg` stays valid; both sides use the one detector so they can't disagree. **53 of 80 diamonds folded** (after recovering the 27 call-headed conds ŌĆö a call-valued cond is fine because capturing `dia_cond = state.regA` READS regA, which the getter treats as consuming the pending call, so the arm's later write won't double-render it; e.g. `return (test_map_cell_bits(arg1, arg2, 194) ? 0 : 1)`, `province_ai_state[x] = (get_province_ai_state(y) ? 5 : 0)`), incl. corrected `return`s + `min_word`/`max_word` now read as real min/max. **KEY: the CFG gate CANNOT see the ternary VALUE** (the contraction is symmetric on raw+structured, so a flipped polarity passes every structural gate ŌĆö the compare-bug blind spot again) ŌåÆ built **`tools/probe-ternary-folds.py`** (runs min/max through the live handler; a polarity flip swaps them) ŌĆö ORACLE-CONFIRMED correct. Gates green: cfg 495/495 + 495/495 (**fallbacks 35 ŌĆö baseline, ZERO regression**), round-trip CLEAN, drift CLEAN, --check 0 BAD, test-vm-cfg 74ŌåÆ86.
  - ­¤¤ó **SHORT-CIRCUIT BOOLEAN REGIONS ŌĆö DONE 2026-06-04 (the multi-predecessor compound conditions).** The 25 multi-pred sites the simple diamond left behind are short-circuit `&&`/`||` chains: a value arm reached from Ōēź2 branch points (e.g. `is_tile_in_bounds`'s `load 0` is the fail-exit of BOTH conditions). `vm_cfg.boolean_regions` detects a KŌēź2 region (K cond blocks + exactly 2 value blocks + 1 merge, single-entry, every branch stays in-region, forward layout); `recover_bool_formula` reconstructs the boolean by recursion over the branch DAG (`formula(block) = (c && reach-true) || (!c && reach-false)` with `_combine_bool` algebraic simplification ŌåÆ a clean chain collapses to `c1 && c2 ŌĆ”`). The decode loop captures each cond at its branch + each value, builds `(formula ? a : b)` at the merge (`_bool_ternary_expr` simplifies `(B?1:0)`ŌåÆ`B`); `bytecode_cfg` contracts the WHOLE region entryŌåÆmerge. **14 regions folded (incl. 2/3/4/6-condition).** `is_tile_in_bounds` = one line `return (arg1<=10 && arg2<=4)`; the 4-cond `$970A` = `return !(x<xmin || x>xmax || y<ymin || y>ymax)` (combat-arena containment). Same gate-blind-spot as the rest ŌåÆ **`probe-ternary-folds.py` gained `is_tile_in_bounds`** as an oracle fixture (a wrong &&/||/negation flips the truth table; ORACLE-CONFIRMED 8/8). Gates green, **fallbacks still 35**; test-vm-cfg 86ŌåÆ94 (region detected / `&&` emitted / witness ~= CONTRACTED / != UNcontracted). **TOTAL value-selection folds now 67 (53 diamond + 14 region); empty-if/else 72ŌåÆ43.** Ō¢Č REMAINING (SAFE honest gotos): 5 boolean regions excluded by single-entry/forward guards + 2 backward-layout diamonds + the cosmetic `if(C){}else{body}` invert / trailing-empty-else drop. - ~~**Extend var-walk to far-frame locals `*(word*)(fp ┬▒ N)`**~~ **PLUMBING + PILOT DONE 2026-06-03.** Subs with >12 locals or odd-aligned slots address spill locals as raw `*(word*)(fp - 38)`. Now nameable end-to-end: (1) **schema** ŌĆö `[vars.bankN."0xADDR"]` accepts quoted far keys `"fp-38"`/`"fp+40"` (`load_var_names` slot_re + `var-walk-apply.py` SLOT_RE + writer quotes them, `+` isn't a TOML bare-key char); (2) **substitution** ŌĆö `apply_var_names` (the existing LAST text-pass at `vm_decompile.py:1065`, NOT render-site ŌĆö keeps it one mechanism, no module global) replaces the whole rendered lvalue: deref `*(word|byte*)(fp - 38)` ŌåÆ `name`, address-of `(fp - 38)` ŌåÆ `&name`; derefs for all keys first, then bare addr, closing-paren-anchored so `fp - 3` can't prefix-match `fp - 38`, and nested derefs resolve inner-first; (3) **guard** ŌĆö `walk_guard.norm_lines` collapses the three far forms to `ID`/`&ID` so a far substitution reads as a pure rename (else the guard false-flags expressionŌåÆidentifier as a logic change). **Pilot:** `draw_daimyo_portrait` ($E76F) 4 spill locals ŌåÆ `pal_idx`/`descriptor_buf`/`descriptor_ptr`/`face_buf`; body now reads as source (`if (pal_idx >= 4) goto`, `syscall16_sram_wrap(8, descriptor_ptr, &descriptor_buf, 4)`, `unpack_composite_face_record(&face_buf)`). **Inert with no far keys (decompiled byte-identical); all gates green** (round-trip 495/45024 CLEAN, --check 0 BAD, drift-guard CLEAN, regen-guard reads it as pure rename). **Census of the SWEEP remaining: ~35 subs / ~77 distinct slots / ~311 refs** ŌĆö bank_00 6/9, bank_01 5/16, bank_02 3/12, **bank_15 21/40** (heaviest: `format_string` 10, `redraw_window` 3; `draw_daimyo_portrait` done). **Two design findings for the sweep Ōåō (next two tickets).** [[project_nobunaga_daimyo_portraits]]

- ~~**EXPORT THE BUILT-IN TEXT FONT (CHR-RAM glyph set)**~~ **DONE 2026-06-02 ŌĆö `tools/render-text.py`.** The font is **bank-0 `$B2BA`** (2bpp CHR; uploaded to CHR-RAM by `render_boot_title_screens $88AC` via `ppu_upload_block_wrap(81,$1000,$B2BA,0)` right before the first menu text is drawn ŌĆö found by reading the title-sequence VM, not the static upload list). CharŌåÆtile = `char_classify $CDCA`, **piecewise** (the font drops some punctuation between ASCII runs, so offsets differ per range): digits `cŌłÆ40`, upper `cŌłÆ43`, lower `cŌłÆ47`, named punctuation explicit. `render-text.py "STRING"` renders any text in the game font (PNG, configurable fg/scale; `--atlas` dumps the glyph set ŌåÆ `atlas/font-glyphs.png`); `from render_text import render_text` for import. **Wired into `build-command-page.py index`** ŌĆö the command numbers + names + "LORD COMMANDS" title on `commands/index.html` are now drawn in the cartridge's own font (45 embedded PNGs). The static hunt below is preserved for the record. [[project-nobunaga-visual-extraction]]
  - *(static-hunt postmortem, kept as a lesson)* goal was: export the cartridge's built-in font (used for ~all nametable text) so we can render labels (e.g. the command-index numbers/names) in the authentic game font. **PIPELINE FULLY DECODED this session:** `format_string $CFFC` (printf-style, builds an ASCII buffer; `%C/%D/%S`, `num_to_ascii $CF98`) ŌåÆ `redraw_window $CEC9` / `char_advance_width $CE81` (putstring) ŌåÆ **`char_classify $CDCA`** maps each ASCII byte ŌåÆ tile index, essentially **`tile = ascii ŌłÆ 40`** (digits '0'=48ŌåÆ8, 'A'=65ŌåÆ25, 'a'=97ŌåÆ57, 'z'=122ŌåÆ82; punctuation via a switch) ŌåÆ glyph blitted from the pattern table via `syscall_ppu_blit_nobank` / `syscall_ppu_blit_from_bank`. So the font occupies **PT1 tiles ~8ŌĆō82** and is **CHR-RAM** (cart is CHR-RAM, iNES byte5=0) uploaded at boot. ŌÜĀ’ĖÅ **STATIC HUNT FAILED** ŌĆö decoded every `ppu_upload_block_wrap(count,dst,src,bank)` site (banks 0/1/2/15): the $1000-dst uploads are all fullscreen graphics ($9D04/$AF64/$B2BA bank6/0 = title/victory screens; $AC4A bank0 = the "KOEI PRESENTS/NOBUNAGA" logo graphic), NOT a clean glyph grid; the font is NOT in a simple block in bank 4 (that's map/terrain tiles). The font likely loads via the **multi-phase `display_fullscreen_graphic_sequence $8003`** or a reset-path loop (`reset_ppu_init $C757` uploads only $30 B = palette). **DO: runtime CHR-RAM capture** ŌĆö `run-animation.py` already has the machinery (`chr_ram = bytearray(0x2000)`, intercepts `PPU_UPLOAD_WRAP $CF7C` with `(bank,src,dst,count)` from the VM stack, `count*16` bytes 2bpp). Build `tools/dump-chr.py`: drive the boot/title/menu init in the emulator, accumulate chr_ram, slice tiles 8ŌĆō82 ŌåÆ the font; then a `render-text.py` that lays a string via `tile=asciiŌłÆ40` for NES-authentic labels. Swap the monospace stand-in in `commands/index.html` (the `.fontnote` block flags this). Reusable "dump CHR-RAM" tool = bonus (helps the strategic-map render task too). - ~~**EMULATOR RNG STUB IS A NO-OP ŌĆö blocks probing every RNG-dependent formula**~~ **FIXED 2026-06-02** (`nobunaga_vm.py` `_syscall_dispatch` task $11). The rng syscall stub advanced an LCG and wrote brk_scratch ($66/$67) but returned `None`, so regL was never set ŌĆö `rng_next_wrapper` (just `push $11; syscall; RETURN`) left a leftover in regL and `rng_mod`'s SIGNED `SMOD` produced negatives (`-13752 smod 10 = -2`). Fix: the stub now returns the LCG value masked to 15 bits (`& 0x7FFF`, non-negative so SMOD yields a clean 0..n-1 for every modulus the game uses Ōēż ~2025). **Verified end-to-end:** `probe-espionage.py` ninja-drain bands now match `{5,10,ŌĆ”,X├Ś5}` exactly across the rng distribution; probe-math32 + run-effect grow unaffected (no rng there). **This unblocks emulator-probing every RNG-dependent formula** (drains, defection size, event spawns, combat rolls). [[feedback_silent_tool_failure_hallucination]]-adjacent: a stub that silently returns None reads as "no input," not "broken."
- **VM CALL frame-arg mapping is REVERSE push order** (confirmed 2026-06-02): the LAST-pushed call arg lands in frame slot `fp+0x0B` = the callee's `operand $0C` ("arg1"). Evidence: the `$8BD0 DEREF` only works on the pointer arg (which is 2nd-pushed) + probe-math32's documented reversal note. **This flipped the bribe contest direction to the intuitive one** (see Now). Keep in mind when hand-reading any multi-arg sub: the decompiler's `local12/local13` are the reverse of source push order. **NOW ORACLE-CONFIRMED 2026-06-02** (executed a real `$E9 CALL`): args are purely stack-passed (zero-copy ŌĆö CALL repoints `fp` so `fp+0x0BŌĆ”` overlap the caller's pushed args; regB is NOT an arg-passing register). Captured during the frame-arg `?` fix (see Now Ō£ģ).
- **Ō¢Č NAMED FRAME VARIABLES ŌĆö "var-walk" / the 3rd sibling (Chris, 2026-06-02)** ŌĆö replace positional `arg1ŌĆōarg4` + `local0ŌĆōlocal11` with semantic names (`fief`, `amount`, `drain_pct`, ŌĆ”). Chris's worry: args live on the STACK, not a static address, so we can't label them like a data table. **Resolution: the name comes from ROLE, not location** ŌĆö recoverable two ways now that pushes are modeled correctly: (a) **usage role-inference** inside the body (`argN->output` ŌćÆ province ptr; `daimyo_record_ptr(argN)` ŌćÆ daimyo idx; `pct_op(argN,ŌĆ”)` ŌćÆ percent); (b) **caller propagation** ŌĆö every call site now shows the real expression pushed into each slot (e.g. callers always push `selected_province_idx` ŌćÆ that arg is a province idx). Same multi-pass back-inference as [[project_nobunaga_label_walk_skill]] / [[project_nobunaga_data_walk_skill]], aimed at frame slots. Storage: per-function arg/local table in `mesen-labels.toml` keyed `(sub, slot)` (e.g. `[args.bank01.$87F0]`); `vm_decompile.py` substitutes like it does sub/data labels. **DEPENDENCY: do the VM-teardown display-order fix FIRST** ŌĆö else caller-propagation maps the pushed expr onto the wrong slot number (reverse-push). `local0ŌĆō11` is the bigger win by volume than args. Pass-2 / post-combat. The "variable naming" limitation noted in [[project_nobunaga_vm_decompiler]] is exactly this.
- **Ō¢Č ENGINE PROVING-GROUNDS (Chris, 2026-06-02, "maybe a test or 2")** ŌĆö two ideas to validate the decompiler/VM toolchain is a real *engine*, not a one-off. (a) **C ŌåÆ bytecode round-trip**: compile the decompiled C back to Sea-16 bytecode, assert byte-identical to ROM ŌåÆ proves the decompiler is lossless + the VM model complete (the ultimate regen-guard). (b) **Cross-game one-shot**: take another KOEI/Sea-16-era title, verify it runs the SAME VM (opcode table/ABI match), then try to one-shot the disassembly with the existing tools. Both are post-pass-1 stretch goals, not committed ŌĆö capture only. Pairs with the VM teardown (a complete opcode model is the prerequisite for both).
- **Ō¢Č END-OF-PROJECT VM TEARDOWN (Chris, 2026-06-02)** ŌĆö register/variable/stack tracking in the Sea-16 VM is "weird and hard to keep track of." Once the subsystems are done, a dedicated **byte-by-byte pass**: every opcode's true semantics ($E8ŌĆō$FF handler set), the full ABI, the **reverse-push display-order quirk** in `vm_decompile.py` (multi-arg calls show `f(c,b,a)`), cleanup of the now-DEAD `recent_pos_writes`/`/*via argN*/` fallback, and any other stateful/mis-modeled opcodes. Seed evidence = this session's oracle traces (`$E9` CALL ABI, `$30ŌĆō$3F`=`PUSH_quick`). Goal: decompiled C that reads naturally with ZERO `?` and no tool round-trips. Spawned from the frame-arg `?` fix, which proved one mis-modeled opcode ($30ŌĆō$3F) was responsible for 996 markers ŌĆö there may be more.
  - **Ō¢Č Task "D" ŌĆö the VM/decompiler WIKI writeup (do AFTER the control-flow structuring epic, so it shows clean `while`/`if`/`switch` C).** **Material sufficiency CHECKED 2026-06-03: abundant ŌĆö every fact captured + cross-checked by Pass 2.** Narrative home already exists (chapters `05-bytecode-vm.md` / `06-vm-disassembler.md` / `08-vm-instruction-set.md` + the `build-*.py`ŌåÆHTML wiki precedent), so D is **NOT greenfield**. Three data tables + two generic blocks now replace them: `_BINOP` (arith/compare/logic/shift-by-reg, with a `none`/`both`/`lhs` signedness-cast field), `_UNARY_A` (inc/dec/shift-by-1/zero-test/negate/deref templates), and `_op_hex`/`_op_int` operand-parse helpers (killed ~14 copies of the `re.search` idiom). **Net ŌłÆ45 lines in `vm_decompile.py`** (ŌłÆ129/+84 incl. tables+comments). - **RUN THE REST OF THE BANKS FOR LABELS** (Chris, 2026-06-01) ŌĆö banks 3-14 are DATA (0 bytecode subs, so /label-walk doesn't apply), but we want named labels we can USE when tracing. Approach: a **/data-walk** sweep over the data banks ŌĆö name the big tables/blobs by the named code that references them (cross-bank pointers like the portrait case: the referencing sub is in bank 0/1/2/15, the data is in bank 3-14). Needs rom-xref to resolve the cross-bank pointer's TARGET bank (the ppu_upload/memcpy_banked bank arg), not assume same-bank ŌĆö that's the limitation the portrait find surfaced. Bank 8 = portrait/face graphics (started). Likely others: map tiles, text/font, sprite/unit graphics, audio (bank 10). Good standing task to make traces readable.
- ~~**PORTRAIT ŌĆö SHELVED 2026-06-01**~~ **RESOLVED 2026-06-01 ŌĆö and the old premise was WRONG.** Historical daimyo's fixed faces do NOT come from a preset base-5 face code in $6EB1 + the composite system. They use a **separate DEDICATED-CHR preset path** (hand-drawn portraits in banks 7-8 via the `$BBD0` descriptor table ŌĆö see the Ō£ģ in Now). `$6EB1` (the base-5 composite code) is written ONLY by `assign_unique_daimyo_face_code` ($DB97) on succession ŌĆö i.e. the composite system is for RNG-generated REPLACEMENT daimyo only, never the canonical roster. The `record[+6]` status byte (0=originalŌåÆpreset, 1=generatedŌåÆcomposite) selects the path. Anthologies rendered: `atlas/daimyo-anthology-{17,50}.png`. [[project_nobunaga_daimyo_portraits]]

- ~~**B7 extended-opcode table ŌĆö CHECK NESDEV FORUMS before deriving**~~ ŌĆö **CLOSED 2026-05-31 (native walk increment 4, no forum needed).** The table is `ext_op_table` ($F263), dispatched by `ext_op_dispatch` ($F246, VM opcode $AB); its ~44 entries point at the 16/32-bit math/logic/bitfield runtime in $EC-$F6, now all named in `mesen-labels.toml` (umul32/udiv32/cmp32/bitfield/etc.). Decoded straight from THIS ROM's disasm ŌĆö the nesdev t=15931 lookup turned out unnecessary. The 3 composite helpers ([[project_nobunaga_math32_cracked]]) remain the formula interface; the individual sub-ops are now readable too for the decompiler's `// TODO:` reduction.
- **Minimal live PPU memory model ŌĆö for the rendering/animation arc, NOT logic** (Chris, 2026-05-30) ŌĆö idea: stop fully stubbing PPU writes and instead keep PPU-side memory live (nametable, palette, OAM, CHR). **Verdict: red herring for mechanics/logic decode** (game logic never reads PPU back; the data path is ROM/SRAM ŌåÆ compute ŌåÆ CPU-RAM *shadow* buffers ($0600 OAM/$0700 palette/$7BFD map staging) ŌåÆ blit syscalls ($01/$14/$0C/$0D) ŌåÆ PPU, and we already intercept at the shadow/staging level ŌĆö PPU is a write-only output sink, only $2002 status is timing, already handled by `wait_for_nmi`). **But genuinely valuable for the *visual* arc.** Two paths to ROMŌåÆMap: **(A)** decode the `$7BFD` staging buffer ourselves ŌåÆ render via the existing metatile renderer (89% working, zero PPU needed ŌĆö use this for the immediate ROMŌåÆMap tool); **(B)** implement a minimal PPU model (2KB nametable + palette RAM + `$2006/$2007` latch + the `$14`/`$01` blit syscalls), run the real render path, and read the final nametable = exactly what the game draws. **Key fact: this cart is CHR-RAM (iNES byte5=0), not CHR-ROM** ŌĆö tile bitmaps are *uploaded* by the CPU, not static in ROM, so pixel-exact rendering LATER (animation chapter) will need to capture CHR-RAM the upload routines produce. **Cheap experiment worth doing before grinding Path A's last 11%:** stand up just nametable + `$2006/$2007` + `$14` blit, run full `$AFE1`, see if the final nametable is a complete map ŌĆö if so, Path B may be the *cleaner* ROMŌåÆMap (reuses `$885E`/`$CC54`'s own metatile expansion). Defer the full model to the animation/display chapter.

- ~~**`native-call-index.py` misses VM-internal bytecode CALL edges**~~ ŌĆö **CLOSED 2026-06-01 (label-walk automation pass).** Root cause was worse than "misses some edges": `VM_HOSTCALL_RE` matched only an **obsolete `host_call` mnemonic (0 occurrences in today's disasm)** instead of the live `CALL_abs`/`CALL_abs_imm1` form (2400+ edges) ŌĆö so the ENTIRE bytecode call graph was absent, which is why every bank_00 batch's verifiers got "0 callers" and recovered via grep, AND why `--by-callgraph` clustering had been silently falling back to ~address order. Fixed `parse_bytecode` (`VM_CALL_RE` matches both forms). Verified: `callers 8377` ŌåÆ `init_daimyo_arms_record ├Ś4`; `stats` shows `call_abs 2415`. Leaves-first clustering is now genuinely call-graph-driven.
- **Data-element labeling via code back-reference ŌĆö the variable-side twin of the label-walk** (Chris, 2026-06-01) ŌĆö the asm dumps carry DATA sections (blobs/tables) that code references; a named function infers its data. E.g. a `play_growth_animation` sub that references `blob_999` Ō¤╣ `blob_999` is the growth animation; that label then propagates to every other referencer (same multi-pass-linker / toml-as-hub trick as the code walk, [[feedback_re_is_multipass_compilation]]). Several hot DATA addrs already queued for labels (Session C list: `$6DA2/$76A9/$6193/$6D2D/$6E4A/$F930-$F95D`).
- **Committed `disasm/*_vm.asm` carry stale per-line annotations for `$40-$4F`** (captured 2026-06-01 during the qimm fix) ŌĆö the `.asm` listings (hand-curated semantic comments, generated by an older tool rev) still show `$46 clearA ; regA = 0 (shared handler $E9F6)`, whereas current `OPCODE_INFO` correctly says `LOADL_qimm` and the handler is `regA = opcode&0xF`. **Cosmetic + the decompiler is immune** (it reads opcode BYTES not the listing mnemonic, see `vm_decompile.py:170-172`), and each line already prints the true `inline operand = N`. The fix is a disasm regen, but that risks losing the hand-curated `; <semantic>` comments ŌåÆ defer until a deliberate disasm-refresh pass. Not blocking anything.

- **Grow-vs-Dam decision rule ŌĆö DERIVE the switch** (Chris, 2026-06-02) ŌĆö now both formulas are exact. Marginal-rice analysis (both feed `output├Śdams` in the harvest): Grow ╬örice ŌłØ `dams ├Ś 10┬Ęamt/ŌłÜoutput`, Dam ╬örice ŌłØ `output ├Ś 2┬Ęamt/ŌłÜoutput` ŌåÆ ratio `5┬Ędams/output` ŌåÆ **crossover at output = 5├Śdams** (Grow below, Dam above; Dam also drain-free while Grow bleeds loy+dams; dams caps 100 so output>500 forces Grow). ŌÜĀ’ĖÅ This SUPERSEDES the older `output┬▓ > 38├Śdams` heuristic in [[project_nobunaga_dam_doctrine]] ŌĆö reconcile + bake the `outputŌēł5┬Ędams` rule into `econ_sim.py` and the doctrine. (Quick win, high strategic value.)
- **Give turn-economy: sell-riceŌåÆgive-gold vs give-rice-direct** (Chris, 2026-06-02) ŌĆö Give treats gold and rice **1:1** (gain depends on quantity, not resource), but the MARKET sells rice at ~2 gold. So: (a) rice is the cheaper "give currency" ŌåÆ give rice directly when you have it; (b) Chris's reverse ŌĆö sell 1 riceŌåÆ2 goldŌåÆgive 2 gold Ōēł ~2├Ś the loyalty ŌĆö is real but costs a TURN + needs the merchant present (turn-economy thesis: 4 slots/yr is the binding constraint, so this usually loses). Model when the merchant+turn cost is worth it; a nice edge case for the optimizer.

>   (UI/scratch helpers) keep positional slots; and **far-frame locals `*(word*)(fp┬▒N)`** (133 refs, mostly bank 15)
>   are NOT var-walk-able today ŌĆö extending the decompiler + `[vars.*]` schema to name them is an Open ticket.
> - **­¤¤ó M4 ŌĆö var-walk (Layer 2) ŌĆö PLUMBING + PILOT DONE 2026-06-03.** The mechanism is built and
>   proven end-to-end on `effect_grow` (bank1 `$87F0`). **Storage:** `[vars.bankN."0xADDR"]` sections in
>   `mesen-labels.toml` ŌĆö one `slot = { name="...", comment }` line per renamed frame slot (the variable-side twin
>   of `[prg.*]`). **Decompiler:** `vm_decompile.load_var_names()` parses them; `apply_var_names()` runs as the LAST
>   emit pass (after `annotate_field_access` et al. form `arg1->output`, so the base just gets renamed ŌåÆ
>   `fief->output`); `decompile-all.py` threads the per-sub dict (module-level `VAR_NAMES`) so `bank_NN.c` AND the
>   merged `all_banks.c` get identical renames. Single-pass word-bounded alternation (no cascade; `local1` can't eat
>   `local11`). **Pilot result:** `effect_grow(word fief, word amount)` with `gain` for the output-gain slot now reads
>   the verified formula as source: `gain = math32_3arg(amount,(6-const_two),sqrt_int(fief->output+amount))<<1; ŌĆ”
>   fief->output += gain; return gain/2;`. **Design rule surfaced + adopted:** ONLY name a slot with ONE coherent role
>   ŌĆö `local10` (reused scratch: headroom, then drain%/2) was correctly LEFT positional as the honest scratch signal.
>   **Guards all green** (isolated M4-only delta = effect_grow alone in both views, pure renames; round-trip 495/45024
>   CLEAN; `--check` 0 BAD; drift-guard CLEAN; `mesen-labels.py` tolerates `[vars.*]`).
>   **NEXT:** crystallize a `/var-walk` skill (3rd sibling to `/label-walk` + `/data-walk`) and fan out ŌĆö
>   `local0-11` is the bigger win by volume than args. Role-inference lanes: (a) usage-role in the body
>   (`argN->output` ŌćÆ province ptr; `pct_op(argN,ŌĆ”)` ŌćÆ percent), (b) caller propagation (the expression each caller

> ### Ō£ģ PRESET DAIMYO PORTRAITS ŌĆö CRACKED + ANTHOLOGY RENDERED 2026-06-01 (`render-portrait.py anthology`)
> The pinned task is DONE. The preset (historical-daimyo) path in `draw_daimyo_portrait` ($E76F, `record[+6]==0` branch) is fully decoded and the two anthologies render NES-exact with names: `atlas/daimyo-anthology-{17,50}.png` (17 + 50 recognizable faces, real palette).
> - **Descriptor table = bank 8 `$BBD0`**, **4 bytes/entry** `{chr_bank, tile_count, src_ptr_LE}`, indexed by `fief_to_mapid(fief)` (the `*4` is the 4-byte stride; the `len=8` syscall copy just over-reads the next entry harmlessly ŌĆö so the "8-byte descriptor" framing was wrong). Self-validating: each entry's `src + count*16` = the next entry's `src`, chaining cleanly. The decompiler's `msg_ng_to_pieces` resolution was the known cross-bank-pointer trap; real table is bank 8.
> - **Portrait CHR packed contiguously in banks 7-8** (mapid 0-28 ŌåÆ bank 7, 29-49 ŌåÆ bank 8). `count` Ōēł 28-35 tiles each.
> - **Layout = bank 8 `$B144`, a PER-PORTRAIT 6├Ś6 tile-index map at `$B144 + mapid*36`** (the bytecode at `$E7E4` computes `fief_to_mapid*36 + $B144` as the blit's map pointer; the blit `ppu_blit_from_bank_wrap` gets bank-arg 8). CHR uploads to `$15B0` = PT1 tile **`0x5B`**, so map cell `v` ŌåÆ uploaded tile `v-0x5B`; `0x5B` = each portrait's background/border filler. ŌÜĀ’ĖÅ **GOTCHA (found via Chris's Miyoshi screenshot):** the map is per-mapid ŌĆö using the FIRST 36 bytes (mapid 0's map) for every portrait renders only Kakizaki correctly and scrambles the rest (face-like but wrong-arrangement = "a couple bad tiles ŌĆ” most tiles bad"). Fixed ŌåÆ all 17+50 match the game.
> - **Palette = `$F7CC`** (bank 15): 4 NES indices `0x3E,0x38,0x28,0x30` (black/cream/gold/white) ŌåÆ BG palette 0.
> - **Names**: bank 3, 9 B/entry ŌĆö 50-fief `$97AB`, 17-fief `$B7AB`. **Mapid mapping**: 50-fief daimyo idx == mapid (identity); 17-fief ŌåÆ `province_to_mapid_table $F70E` `[15,9,13,20,21,17,19,23,22,31,26,27,25,30,32,14,24]`. CROSS-CHECK: 17- & 50-fief Oda both resolve to descriptor[24] (same portrait) Ō£ō.
> - **OPEN (optional):** add `[prg.bank8]` labels for the `$BBD0` descriptor table + `$B144` template + the bank 7-8 portrait CHR region (currently mis-named `msg_ng_to_pieces`/`jumptab_b144`). And the GENERALIZED "render graphics bits from code" tool (below) would subsume this renderer.
> - **GENERALIZED TOOL IDEA (Chris, 2026-06-01): "render graphics bits from code."** A tool that, given an upload/blit call site (or its `(bank, src, count)` args), extracts + renders the CHR it moves ŌĆö code-driven graphics extraction. Would crack the logo, title, map tiles, etc. in one place; the cross-bank bank-arg resolution is the same primitive the parked "run the data banks for labels" sweep needs. High value, reusable. (The portrait renderer is the hand-rolled first instance.)


> ### Ō£ģ THE MAIN TURN LOOP ŌĆö DECODED 2026-06-02 (decode-first; polished format deferred per Chris)
> **`vm_bootstrap $A778` (bank 0) IS the loop**, walked end-to-end & verified vs bytecode (not just the decompiled C). Full writeup: [[project_nobunaga_main_turn_loop]]. Skeleton: init_new_game_state once ŌåÆ **per-season loop**: `ai_strategic_turn_planner $A455` (the tick) ŌåÆ battle-resume block ŌåÆ `spawn_zealot_uprising_force_from_province $A5E6` ŌåÆ resolve staged combat (`call_bank_wrap(2)`) ŌåÆ `shuffle_fief_turn_order_array $A742` ŌåÆ command sub-loop (`call_bank_wrap(1)`ŌåÆ`ai_per_fief_command_driver $B89B`) ŌåÆ game-overŌåÆ`display_fullscreen_graphic_sequence`.
> **3 keystone findings (+ 2 label fixes, regen-guard clean):**
> - **Season-phased economy.** `per_period_fief_daimyo_update_driver $A30D` does `switch(current_season)`: **1**=highwater reset, **2**=`harvest_income_sweep_all_fiefs` (THE harvest, once/yr in season 2 ŌĆö confirms the "fall harvest" memory), **3**=relations decay; aging + natural-death + loyalty-decay-to-90% run EVERY season.

> - **Turn-order array is `$6F1B`, NOT `$6F0B`** ŌĆö the toml label was mis-addressed ($6F0B has ZERO refs). Relocated `daimyo_turn_order` to $6F1B; **fixed a latent bug in `sram-decode-province.py`** (hardcoded the wrong $6F0B). Shuffled each season ($A742), read by command driver ($B918): `selected_province_idx = daimyo_turn_order[ai_per_fief_loop_index]`.
> - **Elegant mechanic ŌĆö the command pass RESUMES across combat.** `ai_per_fief_loop_index $6001` is a persistent global restored into the frame at $B8A4; a mid-pass war saves the index ($B996), bootstrap loops through bank-2 combat, then re-enters and resumes at the next fief. > ### Ō£ģ DECOMPILER FRAME-ARG `?` ŌĆö FIXED 2026-06-02 (ROOT CAUSE = mis-modeled opcode, not a dataflow gap)
> **The "frame-arg ?" turned out to be a one-line semantic BUG, not a heuristic seeding job.** Investigation (oracle-driven, see below) traced ALL of `/*via argN*/ ?` (281) + bare `= ?` (318) + `/*stack underflow*/` (397) ŌĆö **996 markers** ŌĆö to a single cause: the decompiler modeled VM opcodes **`$30ŌĆō$3F` as `storeB_local` (store regB ŌåÆ slot)** when **`OPCODE_INFO` (the semantics authority) says the whole range is `PUSH_quick`** ŌĆö push a frame slot's VALUE onto the data stack (`$30ŌĆō$3B`=push localN, `$3CŌĆō$3F`=push argN, arg-forwarding to a call). The old "store" model both fabricated bogus `argN = ?` assignments AND starved every downstream call of its pushed args (ŌåÆ the underflows). **Fix:** `tools/vm_decompile.py` ŌĆö remapped `$30ŌĆō$3F` to `push_local_neg`/`push_local_pos`, handlers now `state.stack.append(slot_name)`. **RESULT: all 996 markers ŌåÆ 0; net ŌłÆ2058 lines** of decompiled C (the phantom duplicate statements the mis-model produced are gone).
> - **ORACLE-CONFIRMED, not guessed** (`nobunaga_vm` real-stack dumps): executed a real `$E9 CALL` ŌĆö the pushed word lands at new-frame `fp+0x0B`=arg1, NOT regB (kills the "arg1 in regB" red herring; args are purely stack-passed, zero-copy overlap, `adj/2`=argcount). Then single-op traces: `$38` pushes local8 (spŌłÆ=2); `$3C` pushes arg1 (fp+0x0B) ŌĆ” `$3F` pushes arg4 (fp+0x11) ŌĆö matches `local_name('pos')`. `$2CŌĆō$2F` (STORE_quick) are LEFT as real stores (the `arg1=arg1+1` loop-counter at `$CA88` proves they store) ŌĆö only `$30ŌĆō$3F` was wrong.
> - **VALIDATED vs known-good:** `effect_grow` now decompiles to **exactly the verified formula** ŌĆö `math32_3arg(sqrt(o+a),(6ŌłÆskill),amount)` reads (through the decompiler's pre-existing reverse-push display convention) as `ŌīŖamount┬Ę(6ŌłÆskill)/ŌłÜ(output+amount)Ōīŗ`; the old output had `arg2 = const_two` *corrupting the amount* + phantom `local10 = 2` / duplicate `pct_op` lines ŌĆö all gone. The `apply_unit_damage_over_30` loop (bank-2, was riddled with `?`) now reads cleanly (`unit_record_ptr(local8)`, real `local9/10`). Only files touched: `vm_decompile.py` + `decompiled/*.c`.
> - **Tech debt noted:** the `recent_pos_writes` / `/*via argN*/` host_call fallback in `vm_decompile.py` is now DEAD (never populates, never fires) ŌĆö harmless safety net, leave for the teardown. The **reverse-push display order** for multi-arg calls (`math32_3arg(c,b,a)` shows reversed) is a separate pre-existing readability quirk ŌĆö candidate for the teardown, NOT bundled here (would change arg-order interpretation project-wide).
> - **NOT chased (still true): full control-flow STRUCTURING** (the ~1437 gotos ŌåÆ if/else/loop). Genuinely hard; gotos are readable-with-effort; bytecode/emulator settle ambiguity in seconds. [[feedback_transpilation_as_grounding]] [[feedback_re_is_multipass_compilation]] [[project_nobunaga_vm_decompiler]]
> - **Ō¢Č CAPTURED TASK (Chris, 2026-06-02): END-OF-PROJECT VM TEARDOWN.** Register/variable/stack tracking is "weird and hard to keep track of" ŌĆö once the subsystems are done, do a dedicated **byte-by-byte VM pass**: pick apart the Sea-16 VM opcode by opcode + variable by variable (ABI, the full `$E8ŌĆō$FF` handler set, the reverse-push display convention, the dead `recent_pos_writes` cleanup, any remaining stateful opcodes). The oracle traces gathered this session ($E9 CALL ABI, $30ŌĆō$3F PUSH_quick) are the seed evidence. Goal: a decompiler that needs NO `?` and reads naturally without the tools. (See Inbox.)
>
> ### Ō¢Č ARTIFACT (Chris, 2026-06-02): the DAIMYO-ATTRIBUTE reference ŌĆö "what does each stat do" (the daimyo analogue of the skill-level footprint)
> **FIELD MAP DONE this session** (ground-truthed: cross-year save-dump compare fall 1566/1569/1574 + the death-formula code `$9154`). 7-byte record `$752F+idx*7` (names per Chris/manual): **+0 AGE** (monotonic+, death gate Ōēź70), **+1 HEALTH** (declines, /4 in death roll ŌĆö fixes the old "age@+1" error), **+2 DRIVE** (stable, marry-drained, combat-compared $8EB8), **+3 LUCK** (WANDERS ┬▒5/season via `drift_daimyo_luck` $A2ED ŌĆö luck-as-random-walk resolves the old "+3 dropped 105ŌåÆ26"), **+4 CHARISMA** (rises; Train target; income/event/marry; hottest-read), **+5 IQ** (stable, not marry-drained), **+6 portrait/status flag**. > ### ­¤¤Ī COMBAT ENGINE ŌĆö DIVE STARTED 2026-06-02 (spine mapped + the big correction landed)
> The bank-2 combat dive (the last pass-1 subsystem) is **in progress** ŌĆö [[project_nobunaga_combat_engine_decoded]]. Done this session, all vs the clean post-fix C:
> - **Spine mapped.** `battle_init_driver $AFE1` = the **WHOLE battle** (not "per-day" as the old memory said): init ŌåÆ `deploy_both_sides_units_loop` ONCE ŌåÆ **31-day loop** (`run_both_sides_combat_turn(day)` + `apply_unit_damage_over_30`) ŌåÆ resolution. `battle_setup_select_province_phase $AF3B` is **MISNAMED = the battle aftermath/resolution handler** (outcome code ŌåÆ announce ŌåÆ transfer fiefs ŌåÆ conquest); rename candidate.
> - **­¤ö┤ MAJOR CORRECTION (oracle-confirmed, `tools/probe-combat-arena.py`): the "4-quadrant damage formula" was never damage.** `$9675` (renamed `set_combat_arena_rect_by_approach`) sets the **tactical-arena deployment RECTANGLE** `$6FF6-$6FFC` (renamed `combat_arena_x_min/y_min/x_max/y_max`) to the attacker's entry strip by the **compass bearing between the two fiefs' strategic-map coords** (`$B0BA`/`$B0EC` = `strategic_map_fief_x`/`_y`, not attribute tables). Returns an edge code {1=N,2=S,3=W,4=E} consumed by **unit placement**, not damage. Default rect (0,0,10,4)=the 11├Ś5 grid. The `{1,2,4,7}` "magnitudes" were rect coords. `$9B08` (renamed `deploy_both_sides_units_loop`) is the setup deploy pass, not a damage loop. Toml relabeled + regen-guard clean (pure rename). The stale memory [[project_nobunaga_combat_damage_formula_decoded]] is marked Ōøö SUPERSEDED. **Bonus:** caught a decompiler store-annotation bug (vertical branch N/S words swapped) ŌåÆ seed for the VM teardown.
> - **Real model surfaced (static).** Army split into 5 unit-type slots by province composition `$76A9` (`distribute_damage_across_unit_types` is really distribute-MEN). Per-attack casualties = a `rng(6ŌłÆskill)+morale+charisma` contest with a men-capture branch (`resolve_attack_apply_casualties $9E73`), accumulated per-side, applied at `/30`/day (`apply_unit_damage_over_30 $830B`). Combat reads **Charisma + skill** ŌåÆ confirms two daimyo-attribute footprint entries.
> - **Ō£ģ CASUALTY FORMULA EMULATOR-CONFIRMED 2026-06-02 (`tools/probe-combat-casualty.py`).** The attack is a **CAPTURE/DEFECTION CONTEST**, not a kill-counter: `atk_score = rng(6ŌłÆskill)+morale(atk)+charisma(atk_daimyo)` vs `def_score = morale(def)+charisma(def_daimyo)+2┬Ęskill`; if `atk>def`, `pct_op(math32_2arg(atk,atkŌłÆdef), enemy_slot_strength)` men **defect from the enemy's slot to the attacker's slot 0** (cap 9999); on loss/zero, enemy province morale ŌłÆ= skill. **Charisma is the decisive combat stat** ŌĆö in the Oda matchup the attacker won at *every* morale 40ŌĆō120 on charisma alone. Resolved the reverse-push arg binding (body arg1=slot, arg2=men) by internal consistency + the AI caller. Toml `$9E73` annotated; probe registered. **Combat = absorbing the enemy army, not annihilating it.** [[project_nobunaga_combat_engine_decoded]]
> - **Ō£ģ DAMAGE MODEL CLOSED 2026-06-02 ŌĆö THREE decoupled mechanisms (`tools/probe-combat-bleed.py`).** The per-side battle record `$6F7D+6*side = {+0 gold, +2 rice, +4 men}` (the `$8BEA` Gold/Rice/Men triple). **(1) The legendary "/30" is the RICE/SUPPLY clock, NOT damage** ŌĆö `apply_unit_damage_over_30` ŌåÆ renamed **`consume_daily_battle_rice`** ($830B): `rice(+2) ŌłÆ= men(+4)/30` per day ŌćÆ army eats ~men rice over a ~30-day battle, rice 0 ŌåÆ **"you have no rice!"** = the rice-exhaustion/doughnut mechanic + the real "31-day limit." Cross-dump proof: rice drained men-proportionally (ŌłÆ12/ŌłÆ8 = the 32:21 men ratio) while men + `$6FBC` slots held constant. **(2) KILLS** = `apply_pct_reduction_to_unit_strength` ($9D03) via `tally_..._parity_50` ($9DFB): strength-ratio split `local11 = math32_2arg(A,B)=100A/(A+B)`, defender loses `local11%`, attacker `(100ŌłÆlocal11)%`. **(3) CAPTURE** = the morale+charisma contest ($9E73, done above). toml renamed/annotated, regen-guard clean. **This also closes the rice/supply half of Task #4.**
> - **Ō£ģ TERMINATORS + RESOLUTION CLOSED 2026-06-02.** `battle_init_driver`'s 31-day loop exits to `battle_setup_select_province_phase` ŌåÆ renamed **`dispatch_battle_resolution`** ($AF3B) with an OUTCOME CODE that indexes the loser table `battle_conclusion_msgs_loser` ($B640) + observer table `..._observer` ($B650): **3**=day-31 timeout ("your men are exhausted!"), **4**=riceŌēż0 ("supply... out of rice", the `$B06D` SCMPLE on `unit_record+2`=rice), **5**=commander killed (unit **type-0** absent, `check_commander_alive_both_sides` $AB8E, checked after every action), **6**=annihilation (5 escalated when `war_side_state_flag[0]&31`==0); plus retreat ("%s has retreated", Flee). **Unit type-0 = the COMMANDER.** The "You have no rice/soldiers!" strings ($FDEB/$FDFD) are the bank-1 strategic *pre-battle* checks, not tactical terminators. **Aftermath** `apply_conquest_outcome` ($E03C): winner **absorbs BOTH sides' surviving gold/rice/men** into the conquered fief, **ŌłÆ10ŌĆō19% output pillage** (`pct_op(rng(10)+10, output)`), ownership transfer + defeated daimyo's other fiefs neutralized (`province_ai_state=-1`) + `install_new_daimyo`. toml renamed/labeled (incl. the 10 conclusion strings), regen-guard clean. **Task #4 DONE.**
> - **Ō£ģ DAIMYO-ATTRIBUTE COMBAT FOOTPRINT DONE 2026-06-02.** Stats split into two roles: **Charisma drives the damage** (capture contest); **Health/Drive/Luck/IQ drive the AI's engage decision** via `ai_sum_battle_strength` ($8E5D), a weighted attacker-vs-defender stat tally with weights `battle_strength_stat_weights $B5B1` = **[HEALTH 5, DRIVE 10, LUCK 10, CHARISMA 5, IQ 20, morale 10, skill 25]** ŌĆö **IQ (20) is the top daimyo term**, province skill (25) the biggest overall. > **Ō£ģ THE 7 THIN / TURN-SKIP PAGES DONE 2026-06-02** ŌĆö `commands/{pact,marry,rest,grant,map,other,pass}.html` built, every one grounded in its decompiled driver (NO guessing ŌĆö the bytecode arbitrated, and it reclassified the batch). Findings:
>   - **Two are genuinely thin** (no `ui_helper_e80c`, no state write): **`map`** (`driver_map $AF38`, pure strategic-map view, returns 0 ŌåÆ doesn't even spend the turn) and **`pass`** (`driver_pass $B2A1`, a 3-line driver: print "What a waste." ŌåÆ consume the slot).
>   - **`other`** (`driver_other $B23E`) is the **system/options menu**, not a game command: 7 entries via `jumptab_b9e8` / labels `$FF1A` = **Sound / Animat / Wait / Save / Battle / End / Menu** (decoded from ROM). The **Animat** toggle is the master switch for the very command-animation VM the other pages render; **Save** is the only persistence path; only **End** consumes the turn.
>   - **`pact`** (`driver_pact $9C4F`, anim 3) + **`marry`** (`driver_marry $9DC4`, anim 16) are **diplomacy** commands (no formula ŌĆö cost is set by the relations state). Both pay gold to a rival house for an alliance; Marry additionally rolls a **composite bride portrait** (`rng%22+53 ŌåÆ draw_daimyo_portrait`) and, on **refusal, drains the player's OWN daimyo stats** (records +2 / +3 skill / +4 charisma each ŌłÆ1) ŌĆö the only command that snubs you back. Both write the relations matrix (`diplomacy_helper2/3`).
>   - **Chris's reclassification CONFIRMED from code:** **`rest`** (`driver_rest $ADB3`, anim 32) = a **multi-season self-lock** ŌĆö prompt "Seasons" ŌåÆ `number_input(1..10)` ŌåÆ `rest_turns_remaining[daimyo]` ($6D67); the counter gates the daimyo out of actions in Ōēź5 per-turn check-sites across banks 0/1/2. (The recuperation it buys ŌĆö the health write ŌĆö is applied in the per-turn tick, not the driver; pinning that exact write is a small open thread.) **`grant`** (`driver_grant $AF66`, anim 11) = **delegate a fief to AI governance**: sets `province_ai_state[fief]` to one of 6 policies decoded from `$F7D4` ŌåÆ **Home fief / Industrial / Military / Balanced / Farming / Direct** (0 = keep manual control). It's the player's hook into the AI command driver + the same field `neutralize_fief` resets.

The 7 specs added to the `COMMANDS` registry; `commands/README.md` index updated (Rest row promoted from "stub").
> **Ō£ģ MOVE / ASSIGN / VIEW DONE 2026-06-02** ŌĆö three more functional pages, bytecode-grounded:

> **Ō£ģ TRADE DONE 2026-06-02 ŌĆö the merchant subsystem, fully decoded.** `commands/trade.html` built (full subsystem page w/ 6-service table). Findings:

> ### Ō£ģ MERGED PRG-KEYED DECOMPILER VIEW ŌĆö BUILT 2026-06-01 (`tools/decompile-merged.py` ŌåÆ `decompiled/all_banks.c`)
> Chris's readability ask: reading `bank_00.c`, cross-bank refs like `call_bank_wrap(2)`/`call_bank10_entry(1)` are dead ends (defined in bank 15, opaque args), and the switchable `$8000-$BFFF` window means no single flat address space to grep. **Fix:** a new tool emits ONE file (all 4 code banks) keyed by **PRG offset** (`bank*0x4000+(cpu&0x3FFF)`) ŌĆö goto labels `L_pPPPPP`, comments `// PRG $P`, so the same `$8003`-in-two-banks gets distinct identities and ctrl-F a label finds one def. Each named call annotated `// -> bankT $CPU` (follow cross-bank); the entry trampolines resolved to the REAL bytecode entry they JMP into (read from ROM): **`call_bank_wrap(2)` ŌåÆ `bank2 entry battle_init_driver $AFE1`**, `call_bank_wrap(1)` ŌåÆ `ai_per_fief_command_driver $B89B`, `call_bank10_entry(c)` ŌåÆ bank-10 audio `$8003`. 495 subs / ~13.7k lines, **byte-deterministic**, PRG-sorted TOC index at top. **Refactor:** extracted `decompile-all.py::bank_subs()` as the shared core so merged + per-bank C are byte-identical; per-bank `bank_NN.c` UNCHANGED (regen-guard verified) and stay canonical. No def-name collisions across banks (verified). **`decompile-all.py` auto-emits `all_banks.c` on a full run** (`--no-merged` to skip) so the per-bank + merged views regen together and never drift; `decompile-merged.py` also works standalone. Registered in tools/README + CONTEXT quick-routes/artifacts. **Open follow-on (optional):** add `bank1_entry`/`bank2_entry`/`bank10_entry` `$8000` labels to the toml for parity with `bank0_entry` (not needed by the tool ŌĆö it resolves via the ROM JMP target).

> <details><summary>BATCH 1 RESULTS + what the run validated (2026-06-01)</summary>
> **The skill works end-to-end on the oracle-poor bank** (24 agents / 845K tok / ~4.4 min for 3 clusters). Highlights proving the lateral-verify architecture:
> - **`$8003`** AMENDED ŌåÆ `display_fullscreen_graphic_sequence`: verifier caught the proposer citing calls ($BA10/$B9FD/$D134) that **don't exist in bank-0 bytecode** (mis-tiled C), corrected from ground truth.
> - **`$88AC`** AMENDED ŌåÆ `render_boot_title_screens`: verifier **refuted a "marriage screen" inference** (proved `cc35` is a generic 20-caller screen primitive), traced the sub to the boot entry `vm_bootstrap`.
> - **`$9154`** CONFIRMED ŌåÆ `check_daimyo_natural_death`: independently **rediscovered the verified natural-death formula** `(age-10-health/4)/300, ageŌēź70` blind from bytecode = known ground truth reproduced = the method is sound without an oracle.
> - Also named: `verify_sram_save_integrity` ($821E), `transfer_arms_field_pct` ($8377, over $76A9 arms record), `prompt_roll_stat_value`/`prompt_select_scenario_size` (char-gen), `relations_matrix_cell_addr` ($8C35 = arg1*54+arg2+$6193), `clamp_value_to_range`, `calc_year_scaled_random_value`, etc.
>
> **TWO TOOLING FIXES the acceptance run earned (the regen guard / link stage doing its job):**
> - **Decompiler dual-bank fix (`decompile-all.py`).** `$8003` and `$8DE1` stayed anon in bank_00.c after writing the labels. Root cause: a switchable-window CPU address can hold a DIFFERENT function in each bank (`$8003` = `display_fullscreen_graphic_sequence` in bank 0 but `prompt_message_and_redraw` in bank 1 ŌĆö both legit, both in the toml). The old `addrŌåÆbank` map (and flattened `vm.labels`) kept only ONE bank/name per address, shadowing bank 0's label with bank 1's. Replaced `_switchable_label_banks` with **`_switchable_section_labels` ŌåÆ per-(bank,addr) names parsed straight from the toml sections**; each bank's C now uses its own section's name. Verified: bank_00 picks up both names, bank_01.c `$8003` still `prompt_message_and_redraw`, banks 01/02/15 byte-identical. This generalizes the bank_01 walk's `_switchable_label_banks` fix from "exclude other banks" to "select the right bank's name."
> - **`--by-callgraph` leaves-first mode** added to `cluster-anon-subs.py` (call-graph depth via `native-call-index`; roots land in the last batches). Deterministic.
>
> **CAPTURED (Inbox) ŌĆö `native-call-index` misses VM-internal bytecode CALL opcodes** (`$AC CALL_abs`, `CALL_abs_imm1`): nearly every verifier reported "0 callers" for a sub that *does* have a bytecode caller, then recovered it via grep. Teaching the index to parse `CALL_abs`/`CALL_abs_imm1` edges in `bank_NN_vm.asm` would give proposers real call-graph context and cut verifier grep work. **Also noted:** the `[prg.bank1] "0x8DE1"` entry is a dead label (bank_01.c has no sub there; the real `dedup_owners` function is in bank 0) ŌĆö harmless after the dual-bank fix, candidate for the section-cleanup nicety.
> </details>

> ### Ō£ģ BANK-01 WALK ŌĆö COMPLETE 2026-05-31 (57/57 anon named; the orchestration-framework proving ground)
> **DONE in ONE session: pilot (7 subs, hand-run) discovered the framework + fixed a decompiler bug; then the `bank01-label-walk` Workflow named the remaining 50 (19 CONFIRMED / 29 AMENDED / 2 REFUTEDŌåÆ`helper_*`).** `decompiled/bank_01.c` = 0 anon, diff = pure renames (zero logic), other banks byte-identical. Chris's reframe that drove it: don't repeat bank-15's serial coordinator-as-sole-verifier; build a sub-agent pipeline and *work out where verification lives*. Settled empirically (see [[feedback_verification_independence_is_altitude]]):
> - **THE FRAMEWORK:** `propose@decompiled-C ŌåÆ independent-verify@bytecode ŌåÆ root-writes-survivors`. Two lanes: ORACLE (claim maps to a known formula/data-struct ŌåÆ deterministic match, no agent) vs ADVERSARIAL (interpretive ŌåÆ independent refuter at LOWER altitude). Root = single writer + integrator (dedup/collision) + regen guard. Verification flows LATERAL (independent sibling), not UP (rubber-stamp) or SELF (correlated).
> - **Three findings, proven by running it:** (1) **recursion-down is unavailable** ŌĆö Agent-tool sub-agents have no Agent tool, so QA can't be owned by a cluster-lead's children; orchestrate from root or via the **Workflow** tool. (2) **self-QA rubber-stamps** ŌĆö the pilot's self-review CONFIRMED 3 wrong names; an independent verifier that dropped to the bytecode (`vm-disasm.py` + ext-op table + call-index) REFUTED 2/3 + amended the 3rd. (3) **the decompiled C is lossy** (`host_call`s render as `?`/TODO) ŌåÆ the write-gate must be the bytecode level, never the C (even the coordinator can't grade from C ŌĆö I nearly flagged a correct claim as a hallucination).
> - **PILOT NAMES (written, bytecode-verified) `[prg.bank1]`:** `8250 relations_matrix_get` (HIGH, $6193 getter) ┬Ę `8303 math32_muladddiv` (HIGH, floor((a*b+c)/d)) ┬Ę `8271 relations_rng_predicate` (MED, 0/1 OR-of-two-rolls) ┬Ę `8327 scale_div10_capcheck` (MED, overflowŌåÆ-1 sentinel) ┬Ę `8379 apply_two_grows_const1_override` (MED, temp $6D63 2ŌåÆ1 around two grows) ┬Ę `83A2/83D5 province_window_redraw_ba6f/_ba78` (HIGH-struct).
> - **DECOMPILER BUG FOUND + FIXED (the regen guard doubled as a cross-bank-collision detector):** `nobunaga_vm.load_labels()` flattens the toml to `{addr:name}` discarding the `[prg.bankN]` section, so switchable-window ($8000-$BFFF) labels were **bank-blind** ŌĆö bank-1's `$83A2`/`$85A7`/`$8DE1`/`$9323` labels bled onto bank-0/bank-2 code at the same CPU address. Fixed in `decompile-all.py` (`_switchable_label_banks()` + a per-bank filter; ~30 lines, no emulator change). Verified: bank_15 byte-identical, bank_01 = pure +7 renames, bank_00/02 cleaned of the false bleeds (3 audited, all confirmed [prg.bank1]). **Upgrades the old "section-cleanup nicety": the FUNCTIONAL bleed is now fixed in the decompiler; the toml `[prg.bank0]`ŌåÆ`[prg.bank15]` re-sectioning remains a separate cosmetic nicety.**
> - **SCALE RUN (Workflow `bank01-label-walk`, 2026-05-31):** 11 propose agents (clustered by address) ŌåÆ 50 independent bytecode-verifiers, pipelined; 61 agents / 2.5M tok / ~7.5 min. Verifier CORRECTED 29/50 proposer names (the independent-lower-altitude lane earning its keep at scale) and hit known ground truth blind (`B6B4 command_menu_select_loop` ŌĆö the menu loop NOT a scorer; `B79B issue_province_command` via `command_driver_table`; `B89B ai_per_fief_command_driver`; develop-family `891D develop_loyalty`/`896F develop_wealth`/`89C1 develop_morale`). 2 REFUTEDŌåÆhonest `helper_95C9`/`helper_B2EF` (system working as designed). Names + verifier evidence written to `[prg.bank1]` (verdict/confidence flagged). **PROOF: a whole bank, one session, via clustering.**
> - **RECONCILE PASS (pass 2 / "the linker", Workflow `bank01-reconcile`, 2026-05-31)** ŌĆö Chris's framing: this is just multi-pass compilation (scanŌåÆsymbol-tableŌåÆlinkŌåÆtypecheck), the toml IS the symbol table, the bank-bleed was a linkage-scoping bug. Pass 2 walked the call-graph to (a) resolve the 2 REFUTED ŌĆö `helper_95C9 ŌåÆ ai_develop_grow_if_men_exceeds_gold`, `helper_B2EF ŌåÆ ai_calc_men_surplus_over_gold_and_rice` (their callers are the now-named `ai_develop_*` handlers) ŌĆö and (b) re-check field-semantic names. **It also caught a COORDINATOR error:** I had mis-"corrected" the province field map (flipped it to the ROM-defaults `header`@+0 layout). The reconcile agents anchored on the *empirically verified* `effect_grow`ŌåÆoutput@+8 and refused the bad premise ŌåÆ the live `$7001` map (`gold`@+0ŌĆ”`header`@+24, = `vm_decompile.PROV_FIELDS`) was right all along; the 57 names stand. Doc fix reverted + the two-table distinction now documented in commands/README + CONTEXT. Lesson: the verifier checks the *orchestrator* too, not just proposers ([[feedback_verification_independence_is_altitude]]). **STILL OPEN:** what `header`/base-koku is exactly and how runtime koku (w/ randomness) derives from it ŌĆö a walk item.

- **NAMING / CONTEXT PASS on the decompiled C ŌĆö LAYER 1 DONE (2026-05-30).**
>   1. **[x] Mechanical propagation (deterministic) ŌĆö DONE 2026-05-30.** `vm_decompile.py` now names a function from its `mesen-labels.toml` label at the *definition* (header + `word <name>(...)` decl) and as a *call-site fallback* (when the disasm operand has no inline `(label)`). Threaded the labels dict through `decompile-all.py` and the standalone CLI; added `_label_name()` (accepts addrŌåÆname or addrŌåÆ(name,comment), sanitizes to a valid C ident). Regenerated all 4 banks: **115/495 definitions now named** (bank_01 economy 72/131, bank_15 kernel 37/135, bank_02 combat 4/131, bank_00 2/98 ŌĆö combat/bank_00 are still anonymous = Layer 2 territory). Verified: diff is **100% renames** (zero logic change), re-run is **byte-identical** (determinism preserved). `effect_grow`/`effect_tax`/`effect_war_a`/`fief_info_display`/ŌĆ” now read directly.
>   2. **Ō¢Č NEXT ŌĆö Analytical naming (the deep-dive):** name the still-anonymous subs (the 380 remaining `sub_XXXX`, concentrated in **bank_02 combat** 127/131 and **bank_00** 96/98) by reading behavior ŌĆö which province fields they touch (`->loyalty`, `->men`), which host-calls they make, who calls them (call-graph from the `CALL_abs`/`host_call` edges). Each newly-understood sub gets a label added to `mesen-labels.toml`, which **propagates back via Layer 1 on the next regen** ŌĆö a compounding loop. Also the lever that lowers the 22% `// TODO:` (decoding an opcode's semantics + naming the subs that use it go together). The call-graph driver `tools/driver-call-index.py` **EXISTS** (confirmed 2026-05-30) ŌĆö use it to build the who-calls-whom map. Start with bank_02 (combat ŌĆö feeds the parked deserter/spoils + AI-war-scorer questions; lowest named-coverage so highest marginal value).
- **Ō¢Č NEW EPIC (2026-05-31) ŌĆö NATIVE-CODE FUNCTIONAL LABELING, top-down readability.** Chris's framing: most code is decompiled but carries auto labels (`sub_XXXX`/`b15_cXXXX`), so it's hard to read/find; the apparent "orphans" at `$C000+` (e.g. `$C537`, `$C54F`, `$C567`, `$C570`) **already have good toml names** ŌĆö they just weren't propagated into the disasm/call-sites. Method: walk code linearly ŌåÆ assign FUNCTIONAL labels (what it touches / how it ends) ŌåÆ then work BACKWARD via the call-graph to refine functionalŌåÆpurpose names; recursive, divisible into address-range tasks. **The toml is the single propagation hub** ŌĆö label once, it flows to every consumer.
>   - [x] **KEYSTONE BUILT 2026-05-31: `tools/mesen-labels.py` projector** (see Open/Done). `--mlb` loads labels into Mesen; `--asm` names the native disasm (bank 15: 188 call-sites de-anonymized, `jsr b15_c537` ŌåÆ `jsr wait_vblank`); `decompiled/*.c` already reads the toml. This is the native analogue of the VM decompiler's Layer-1 mechanical propagation ŌĆö the missing piece that makes "label one sub ŌåÆ document all its callers" actually work.
>   - [x] **`tools/native-call-index.py` BUILT 2026-05-31** ŌĆö who-calls-whom + true-orphan finder, FUSING native jsr/jmp + bytecode host_call + ROM dispatch tables (syscall/vm-opcode/command) + vectors (a jsr-only graph would flag ~50 false orphans). `callers <addr>` / `calls <addr>` / `orphans [--bank N] [--named-only]` / `stats`. Validated: `callers C537` ŌåÆ reset_handler ├Ś2 + ppu_safe_gate; only **13 named orphans, all legit** (data tables, indirect-reached `vm_bootstrap`/`battle_init_driver`/`music_*` via `jmp ($0068)`, + dead `ui_unused`). Deterministic. ŌÜĀ’ĖÅ blind to unresolved indirect jmps ŌĆö those surface AS orphans (correct signal: "needs indirect resolution").
>   - **PHASE 0 (TOOLING) COMPLETE 2026-05-31 ŌĆö ready to walk.** Both keystones built (projector + call-index). The projector also handles **variables/arrays**, not just functions: `mesen-labels.toml [ram]` + `--asm` already name the `LDA $base,Y` idiom (base named, index kept) and absolute zero-page accesses (incl. the `hex 8d 73 00 ; sta $0073` comment form ŌĆö bug-fixed 2026-05-31; immediates `#$XX` protected). So bare `$XXXX` operands now = a **coverage gap to fill during the walk**, same loop as functions. Common loop: pick a range/cluster ŌåÆ walk linearly, assign FUNCTIONAL labels (memory/regs/syscalls touched, exit shape) ŌåÆ add to `mesen-labels.toml` ŌåÆ `py tools/mesen-labels.py --mlb --asm` to propagate ŌåÆ `native-call-index.py callers <addr>` backward pass to refine functionalŌåÆPURPOSE names.
>   - **TWO SEPARATE WALKS (Chris, 2026-05-31) ŌĆö same toml hub, different surfaces:**
>     1. **NATIVE 6502 walk** ŌĆö read `disasm/bank_NN_named.asm` (projector output) + `native-call-index.py`. **First target: bank 15 kernel `$C000+`** (`orphans --bank 15` + linear read of `bank_15_named.asm`). Labels land in toml `[prg.bank15]` (kernel) / `[ram]` (vars). Then banks 0/1/2 native portions. This is the walk the call-index + projector were built for. *(The decompiler is blind to native code, so this is the only way to read it.)*
>        - **WALK STARTED 2026-05-31 ŌĆö syscall dispatch table fully decoded.** Read the 23-entry `syscall_dispatch_table` ($C173) byte-for-byte from ROM (via `bank_15_named.asm` hex). 18 ids = real handlers (already labeled); id $00 -> reset_handler ($C000, a soft-reset syscall); ids **$02/$0B/$0E/$0F are NO-OP stubs** (JMP straight to an RTS) at $C34B/$C427/$C535/$C536 ŌĆö now labeled `syscall_noop_02/_0b/_0e/_0f` and propagated via `py tools/mesen-labels.py --mlb --asm`. This closes the "unnamed syscall handlers" item in Open (only the no-op SEMANTICS-by-task-id-caller lookup remains, deferred). **ŌÜĀ’ĖÅ TOOLING LESSON:** `python` is NOT on PATH on this box ŌĆö it silently fails ("Python was not found"), and the failed command's "output" came back as hallucinated bytes that nearly corrupted the labels. **Use `py -3` for all scripts.** First attempt's bogus edits (a fake `$C148` table + an `irq_handler` move) were caught and reverted. **Ō¢Č NEXT: `py tools/native-call-index.py orphans --bank 15`, then linear-read `bank_15_named.asm` from the next unnamed cluster.**
>        - **WALK INCREMENT 3 + REAL BLOCKER FOUND (2026-05-31) ŌĆö the disassembler never anchored the jump-table-reached handlers; the projector can't rename a label that isn't there.** Continuing linear from $C7xx, the call-index flagged `b15_c238` / `b15_c4b5` as "unnamed subs" ŌĆö but reading the bodies shows they are NOT functions: `b15_c238` is the inner copy LOOP head inside `syscall_memcpy_banked` ($C22C) and `b15_c4b5` is the inner write LOOP head inside the PPU-blit syscall ($C428/$C437). They (and the syscall ENTRIES themselves) read anonymous because the syscall handler labels aren't reaching `bank_15_named.asm`: `grep -cE "^syscall_" bank_15_named.asm` = **8** of **24** toml syscall_ labels. **RESOLVED 2026-05-31 ŌĆö anchor-insertion added to `mesen-labels.py`.** `--asm` now INSERTS a `name:` anchor on any line whose trailing `; 3XXXXX:` PRG-offset matches a toml FIXED-bank ($C000-$FFFF, address-authoritative) label that lacks an anchor; exact line-start match auto-excludes VM-bytecode subs (e.g. math32_3arg $D6B8 sits mid-`hex`-line, so it is NOT anchored ŌĆö correctly, it's the decompiler's domain). Fixed-bank ONLY by design ŌĆö the switchable $8000-$BFFF window stays untouched until the section cleanup (a wrong section there would anchor the wrong bank's code). Added `--dry-run`. **Verified, idempotent: 36 anchors inserted** ŌĆö the syscall handler entries (8ŌåÆ**23** `syscall_` anchors; the 24th, syscall16_sram_wrap $CBBD, is bytecode-reached mid-hex-line so correctly skipped), the VM-opcode handlers (`vm_op_*` 0ŌåÆ6), music (0ŌåÆ4), + a few helpers. The syscall/blit call-sites + their inner loop heads (`b15_c238` etc.) now read in-context with the entry named above them. **CORRECTION to my own mid-session claim:** this did NOT drop the "29 unnamed jsr-targets" ŌĆö those 29 are a DIFFERENT set (genuinely unlabeled functions not yet in the toml); the 36 anchors were table-reached entries (syscall/vm-op), which aren't jsr'd. The bank0/[prg.bankN] mis-section is confirmed a pure NICETY (nmi_off lives in [prg.bank0] yet applies fine ŌĆö the tool address-normalizes). **Ō¢Č NEXT: walk the 29 still-unnamed jsr-targets** (`grep -oE "jsr b15_[0-9a-f]{4}" disasm/bank_15_named.asm | sort -u` ŌĆö the high-kernel $ECDBŌĆō$F669 cluster feeds the C layer; the $C7xxŌĆō$C9xx cluster is the audio engine), then the section cleanup as prep for the bank-0 walk.
>          **ROOT CAUSE (corrected ŌĆö my first commit 8c1f71e guessed "bank0 section shadows bank15", which is WRONG and is fixed here):** the projector only *renames* existing `b15_XXXX:` anchors in the plain disasm. CONFIRMED 3 ways (Grep+py+PowerShell agree): at $C54F (nmi_off, WORKS) the plain `bank_15.asm` line 610 already has the anchor `b15_c54f:`; at $C22C (memcpy, FAILS) line 247 is a BARE instruction with no `b15_c22c:` anchor. The syscall handlers are reached ONLY through the `$C173` JMP table (indirect), so the recursive-descent disassembler never marked them as code entry points ŌåÆ no anchor exists ŌåÆ nothing for the projector to rename. The `[prg.bank0]` mis-section is NOT the cause (nmi_off lives in `[prg.bank0]` and DID get applied ŌåÆ section is purely cosmetic; the projector address-normalizes, exactly as its own warning says). So the bank0 cleanup stays a genuine *nicety*, de-escalated back from "critical path".

>       **SESSION C ŌĆö COMPLETE 2026-05-31 (coordinator + 5-agent read fan-out; the analytical Layer-2 walk). bank-15 BYTECODE library is now 100% named.** All **93** remaining anonymous bytecode subs in `$CA03-$E6B9` named in `mesen-labels.toml [prg.bank15]` ŌåÆ `decompiled/bank_15.c` now has **0 anonymous `sub_XXXX` definitions** (135/135 named; was 42). Method: coordinator read the artifact for verification context + chunked the 93 into 5 address-range clusters ŌåÆ 5 read-only general-purpose agents proposed names+evidence+confidence from the C bodies + `native-call-index` call-graph ŌåÆ coordinator spot-verified every HIGH claim against the actual C (and against known data labels), accepted MED with honest comments, downgraded LOW guesses to structural `*_helper_XXXX` names. Each toml entry carries an inline `[HIGH]/[MED]/[LOW]` flag. Propagated via `py -3 tools/mesen-labels.py --mlb --asm` + `py -3 tools/decompile-all.py`; **re-run byte-identical (md5 `96482e33`), determinism preserved.**
>       - **What the library turned out to be:** a libc-style runtime (`is_digit`/`strlen`/`strcmp`/`strcpy`/`memchr`/`to_upper`/`min`/`max`/`swap_*`), number I/O (`num_to_ascii`/`atoi_decimal`/`format_string` = the `%C/%D/%S` printf), input (`poll_input` $D14E confirmed = the controller state-machine, `wait_button_edge`), PPU-syscall wrappers (`ppu_upload_block_wrap`/`palette_write_wrap`/`ppu_render_rect_wrap` ŌĆö 30/33/21 callers), record accessors (`daimyo_record_addr` $D7CD = `idx*7+$752F`, `get_province_ai_state`/`province_ai_state_addr` over $6CF7), and the **conquest/territory-transfer machinery** (`apply_conquest_outcome` $E03C orchestrator + `reassign_fiefs_to_conqueror`/`install_new_daimyo`/`init_new_daimyo_province_stats`/`clear_fief_pair_6193`).
>       - **BONUS CRACK ŌĆö daimyo NAME GENERATOR found.** `$DCB2 generate_daimyo_name`: RNG-picks a row from each syllable table (`$F930`, `$F95D`), concatenates, and rejects duplicates against `daimyo_name_table` ($77A8) via `strcmp` ŌĆö exactly the regenerator the $77A8 comment hypothesized (explains the garbled-name displacement artifacts like 'Sate\0ui').
>       - **Compounding payoff confirmed:** the hot leaves now resolve at call-sites across ALL banks ŌĆö `get_province_ai_state` 52 refs, `daimyo_record_addr` 50, `fief_to_daimyo_record_addr` 41, `poll_input` 15. Bank-0's callees are now self-documenting (leaves-before-roots achieved).
>       - **(1) OPCODE-SEMANTIC DECODE ŌĆö DONE 2026-05-31 (the last stop in the bank-15 task).** Read the undecoded VM-opcode handler bodies ($EA11-$EB25, named in Session B) and added rendering cases to `vm_decompile.py`. **TODO lines across all 4 banks: 698 -> 10 (98.6% cleared).** What got decoded: the general FRAME-LOCAL ops (all `vm_fp + signed offset`, from the `vm_addr_ptr2_plus_{sbyte,word}` handlers) ŌĆö `$81/$82` word-load->A, `$83/$84` word-load->B, `$85/$86` store-A->word (Ō£ō matches the combat-damage-writer memory), `$87/$88` push-word, `$A0-$A3` byte load/store/push, `$90` add-imm16, `$DE/$DF` frame-address, `$50` setB=0; PLUS the missing comparison/arith MIRROR cases that were never in the elif chain (`cmp_sge`/`cmp_ugt`/`cmp_ult`/`is_zero`, `div_unsigned`/`mod_unsigned`/`bitxor`/`lshr/ashr_by_regB`/`pushA_B2`) ŌĆö these alone gutted bank_02 combat (223->1); and the byte-memory mirrors `loadA_mem_byte`/`storeA_mem_byte`. New `vm_decompile.py` helpers `_WORD_SLOT`/`frame_word/byte/addr`/`_signed_operand` render frame access as `localN` when the offset hits a standard word slot (vm_fp-24..-2) else an explicit `*(word*)(fp - N)`/`(fp + N)`. **Verified:** re-run byte-identical (determinism preserved); quality-read confirms faithful output ŌĆö `cursor_nav_loop` now reads as a local word-array cursor (`local6[local5]`), `format_string` reads as a clean printf parser (`*(byte*)(fp-1)` char, `==37`='%', `==46`='.', `is_digit`/`atoi_decimal`).
>       - **FOLLOW-UP ŌĆö last 10 TODOs cleared, 698 -> 0 (commit pending).** The "10 survivors" split into 3 cases on inspection: **(a) `op_CB` = `regA = -regA`** (16-bit negate, handler $EF09) ŌĆö one-line case. **(b) `host_call_indirect`/`_simple` ($EA/$DD) = call through a computed pointer in regA** ŌĆö render `(*(callee))(args)`, arity from the $EA ptr1-adjust byte (now reads e.g. `(*(local10))(...)`). **(c) `op_FF` was NOT an opcode ŌĆö it was a `vm-disasm.py` LENGTH BUG.** `op_FF`'s handler at $EF93 is `hex 00` (a BRK trap); 4 traps can't be live code. Root cause: ext_op **$18/$19 = `load_a32/b32_from_ptr3`** read a **4-byte inline immediate** from the bytecode (advance ptr3 by 4, handlers $F4F4/$F500), but `instr_len` gave `B7` a fixed length 2, so the immediate's bytes got decoded as opcodes (a 32-bit `0xFFFFFFFF` surfaced as four `$FF` traps). **Fixed `instr_len`: `$B7` with index $18/$19 = length 6.** This corrected **6 sites** (bank1├Ś5, bank15├Ś1) ŌĆö only one had produced visible `op_FF`; the other 5 were SILENTLY mis-decoding their tails. Decompiler now renders the imm32 into regA/regB ($18->A, $19->B). Tiling still 0 BAD on all 4 banks; re-run byte-identical. **The decompiler's `// TODO:` was a working bug-detector ŌĆö it surfaced a disassembler correctness bug, exactly the "drop a level when the abstractions disagree" discipline.** **Ō£ģ BANK-15 TASK COMPLETE** (Sessions A+B+C + opcode-decode: native handlers named, all 135 bytecode subs named, opcode semantics rendered). **(2) Ō¢Č THE BANK-0 WALK is now the frontier** ŌĆö the high-level turn/AI logic, sitting on a fully-named + fully-rendered bank-15 substrate (the actual destination). Bank-0 = 96/98 anon, bank-2 combat = 127/131 anon (same 5-agent fan-out method as Session C).

## Open ŌĆö questions & blockers
- **6 syscalls still TODO** (auto-stubbed + logged in `nobunaga_vm.SYSCALLS`; resolve when a run needs one ŌĆö `probe-map-emit.py` flags TODO syscalls that fire): `$00`, `$02`, `$0B`, `$0E`, `$0F` (**handlers now labeled 2026-05-31**: $00->reset_handler ($C000, soft-reset); $02/$0B/$0E/$0F = `syscall_noop_*` RTS no-ops at $C34B/$C427/$C535/$C536 ŌĆö so these are no-op syscalls, nothing to emulate; only their bytecode callers-by-task-id remain a curiosity), `$16` sram_block_checksum (`$C5AA` ŌĆö save I/O + MMC1 `$BFFF` WRAM gates; emulate the copy+checksum, skip the gates). NOTE: table is **23 entries** (ids 0-22), not 32 ŌĆö "32" likely counts bytecode wrappers (e.g. `rng_next_wrapper $CA46`) or a nesdev superset; verify against nesdev t=15931 if the discrepancy matters.
- ~~**`$07` call_bank**~~ ŌĆö **DONE 2026-05-30.** Implemented in `nobunaga_vm` (`_run_native_call`): mirrors native `$C339` (save bank / `switch_bank(struct[sp+2])` / run the bank's native `$8000` entry / restore). The `$8000` entry trampolines via `$E823` (`vm_entry`) into inline VM bytecode, which is run through a re-entrant dispatcher loop so ITS `$F226` syscalls hit the python kernel layer (not the MMC1-dependent native handlers). Returns clean, balances vm_sp (╬ö=0), preserves the frame. In the AFE1 battle-init the call targets bank 10 (audio) ŌĆö effect is headless-moot, but it no longer derails the caller's `vm_return`.
- ~~**`math32_3arg` / `math32_2arg` ext-opcodes**~~ ŌĆö **CRACKED 2026-05-29** via `tools/probe-math32.py` (emulator probe, all vectors matched): `pct_op(a,b)=ŌīŖab/100Ōīŗ`, `math32_3arg(a,b,c)=ŌīŖab/cŌīŗ`, `math32_2arg(a,b)=ŌīŖ100a/(a+b)Ōīŗ`. The ~47-entry B7 ext-op table was NOT decoded and didn't need to be ŌĆö these 3 composite helpers are the interface every formula calls. **Now unblocks** (downstream refinements): exact **Dam constants**, the **AI war scorer** magnitudes, remaining **combat** magnitudes, and a re-check of the grow-drain factor (math32_2arg gives `100┬Ęgain/(gain+output)` ŌĆö twice the empirical `50┬ĘŌĆ”` fit; verify how the grow handler scales it).
- **Dam formula** ŌĆö partial; output-coupling derived, exact constants pending (needs the ext-op unlock or a clean isolated test). See [commands/dam.md](./commands/dam.md).
- **Combat damage** ŌĆö 2 of 4 quadrants confirmed via Lua; 2 remain. See ch17 + [[project_nobunaga_combat_damage_formula_decoded]].
- ~~**AI war scorer** (`sub_B6B4` via `$B79B`)~~ ŌĆö **LARGELY CRACKED 2026-05-30** (see the Now-section AI-war entry). `sub_B6B4` was mis-IDed as the scorer (it's the shared menu loop); the real war-target choice is the bank-0 planner's `ai_war_target_flags[$6DD4][i] |= rng_mod(400) < (100ŌłÆhealth)`. RNG-weighted-eats-the-weak confirmed in code. Remaining: pin the planner's loop index + decode `$D5/$D9` SWITCH opcodes. See [[project_nobunaga_ai_war_architecture]].
- ~~**`mesen-labels.py` missing**~~ ŌĆö **BUILT 2026-05-31** (`tools/mesen-labels.py`).
