- ~~**`vm-disasm.py` missing**~~ ŌĆö **RECOVERED 2026-05-30** (`tools/vm-disasm.py`). See Done + the reframed EPIC.

### EPIC: DREAM STRUCTURER ŌĆö pattern-INDEPENDENT gotoŌåÆreadable C (Chris, 2026-06-07; NEW ACTIVE FRONTIER)
> **SAME GOAL as the V2 region reducer (readable, goto-minimal C), a FUNDAMENTALLY DIFFERENT METHOD.** This is not a tune of V2 ŌĆö it's a parallel `tools/dream.py` fork built on a different theory of structuring. We stopped grinding V2's atom residue (829 gotos) and are testing whether the DREAM approach reaches readable C *without* the per-shape atom hunt.
>
> **SOURCE:** Yakdan, Eschweiler, Gerhards-Padilla, Smith. **"No More Gotos: Decompilation Using Pattern-Independent Control-Flow Structuring and Semantics-Preserving Transformations." NDSS 2015.** The DREAM decompiler.
>
> **THE TWO METHODS, side by side:**
>   - **V2 (`vm_reduce.py`) ŌĆö pattern-matching region reducer.** Matches CFG subgraphs against a catalog (~7 base rules + a growing atom table of inverse-lowerings), applied to a fixpoint. Each unhandled shape is a *missing atom* ŌåÆ the convergence path is "name the forward lowering, add its inverse" ([[decompiler-bottom-up-thesis]], [[decompiler-atom-log]]). Needs the [[lowering-atlas]] as a **compiler reference** (which shapes the NA1 compiler actually emits). Currently canonical/default; **V2 = 829 gotos**.
>   - **DREAM (`dream.py`) ŌĆö pattern-INDEPENDENT condition-based structuring.** Computes a **reaching condition** for each node (a boolean formula over branch predicates), then refines those formulas directly into `if/else/switch/loops`. **Goto-free by construction** (B├ČhmŌĆōJacopini) ŌĆö there is no shape catalog to be incomplete, so there is no atom residue. **Compiler-INDEPENDENT**: it derives structure from the boolean logic of the CFG, not from "what did this compiler emit," so it needs no compiler reference and the lowering-atlas transfers as a *pure readability oracle* rather than a correctness crutch.
>   - **WHY TRY IT:** V2's residue is, by construction, a tail of rare per-shape atoms (each clears a few subs). DREAM's bet is that a single condition-refinement engine subsumes the whole tail at once ŌĆö the closure property V2 chases shape-by-shape is *inherent* to reaching conditions. The risk it trades for: condition formulas can blow up / read worse than a clean pattern match, which is exactly what the paper's semantics-preserving simplification transforms + the readability oracle are there to control.
>
> **RELATIONSHIP TO V2 (locked):** DREAM is a **fork running in parallel**, NOT a replacement. V2 stays the canonical structurer and the default `decompiled/*.c` source. DREAM proves itself on the SAME corpus, through the SAME CFG-equivalence gate (`structured_equivalent` + the `--raw` witness), and only displaces V2 if it folds **Ōēź V2 with every gate green and reads as good or better.** The lowering-atlas is the readability tie-breaker. Until then both live side by side; no V2 code is deleted.
>
> **STATUS ŌĆö PoC FOUNDATION BUILT + GROUND-TRUTH VERIFIED (commit `a5f311e`, branch `dream-structuring`). Does NOT yet emit structured C.** What's in `tools/dream.py` (260 lines):
>   1. **Boolean layer** ŌĆö immutable canonical expr tuples (`T`/`F`/`lit`+polarity/`and`/`or`); `_and`/`_or` with complementation (`x&!xŌåÆF`), absorption, idempotence; De Morgan `neg`; `to_c` renderer.
>   2. **`tagged_cfg()`** ŌĆö reuses `vm_cfg` + `vm_reduce._parse_block` to recover, per edge, the branch predicate Žä(u,v) it's taken under. **VERIFIED against the asm on `char_classify`.**
>   3. **`reaching_conditions()`** ŌĆö cr(h,n) = OR over preds v of cr(h,v) & Žä(v,n), in **reverse-postorder** (topological for the acyclic graph; a real address-orderŌēĀtopo-order bug was caught + fixed here per paper ┬¦IV-B). **VERIFIED** ŌĆö re-derived the "lowercase"/"uppercase" byte-range conditions straight from the raw compares.
>   4. **`_capture_sub()` harness** ŌĆö grabs one sub's `(lines, instructions)` via the `structure_v2` hook from `decompile-all`, so a single sub can be dumped: `py -3 tools/dream.py <bank> <sub_addr_hex>` (e.g. `tools/dream.py 15 CDCF`). Front-end (bytecodeŌåÆCFG, per-block C, predicates) is **inherited** from `vm_cfg`/`vm_decompile`/`vm_reduce`; DREAM replaces ONLY the structuring step.
>
> **PROGRESS ŌĆö ALL 6 RUNGS DONE + bake-off won + post-bake-off polish (2026-06-10).** Final corpus: **DREAM OWNS 479/495 (96.8%)** = 468 fully goto-free + 11 idiomatic-goto (re-shared); **V2 384/495 goto-free (77.6%), 808 gotos**; DREAM strict-wins 85 subs (erasing 465 V2 gotos). Plus a corpus-wide **value-correctness fix** (`value_merge_phis`, 91 subs incl. the key `$A45A` ŌĆö V2 had it structurally right but value-WRONG). Remaining 16 V2-fallback = 1 over-dup + 1 reject + 14 hard loops. Gates green, deterministic. **Ō¢ČŌ¢Č NEXT SESSION: EXECUTE THE CUTOVER ŌĆö "fold DREAM in, make it the code oracle" (see the cutover plan in the rung-6 entry below).** Rung 1 (acyclic if/else) Ō£ģ, rung 2 (condition-aware + switch) Ō£ģ, rung 3 (loops: while/do-while/nested/multi-exit) Ō£ģ, rungs 4ŌĆō5 (irreducible handling + simplifier, folded into the above) Ō£ģ, **rung 6 (bake-off + cutover decision) Ō£ģ ŌĆö verdict: displace V2 as PRIMARY, retain V2 as FALLBACK for the 24-sub hard tail.** **Ō¢Č LEVER #1 (idiomatic-goto re-sharing) Ō£ģ DONE 2026-06-10 (cont.):** `_reshare` keeps a shared over-dup sink ONCE under a label + `goto`s from the rest (gate-validated like break/fallthrough). **Over-dups 7 ŌåÆ 1; DREAM now OWNS 477/495 (471 goto-free + 6 idiomatic-goto); V2-fallback set 24 ŌåÆ 18**, no regression. **Ō¢Č REMAINING (~3.6%, toward a FULL cutover):** (a) hard-tail loops (the 16 passthrough ŌĆö multi-level-break / irreducible), (b) the `$A45A` continuation-HOIST (its over-dup is a loop continuation ŌåÆ pull out after the if = goto-free; harder than re-sharing) + the `$E041` reject, (c) EXECUTE the cutover wiring (DREAM-emit + V2 fallback writing `decompiled/*.c`) when the decision is to be *performed*, not just *recorded*.
>
> **Ō¢ČŌ¢Č NEXT SESSION ŌĆö EXECUTE THE CUTOVER ("fold DREAM in ŌåÆ the new code oracle"). PLAN:** make DREAM the PRIMARY structurer that writes the canonical `decompiled/*.c`, with V2 as fallback for the ~16 it doesn't own. **(1)** New emit driver (in `decompile-all.py` or a thin wrapper): per sub, try DREAM (`dream_ast` ŌåÆ `_emit_ast`, then `_reshare` if over-dup) and use it IFF the AST-native gate passes (`dream_equivalent_ast`) and dup Ōēż `DUP_CAP`; ELSE fall back to V2 (`vm_reduce`) ŌĆö same front-end lines, so the `value_merge_phis` temps are already in both. **(2)** `STRUCTURE_DREAM` flag mirroring `STRUCTURE_V2`; write `decompiled/bank_NN.dream.c`, spot-read, then promote to canonical `*.c`. **(3)** Gate the hybrid: DREAM subs via `dream_equivalent_ast`, V2-fallback subs via `structured_equivalent`; keep 114-suite + V1+V2 495/495 + stack-audit green + deterministic. **(4)** Result = the **code oracle**: one canonical readable-C view, DREAM where it wins (479/495), V2 where it doesn't, value-correct throughout. **WATCH-OUTS:** `_reshare` currently runs only in `_check`/`_emit_one` ŌĆö the cutover emit path must call it; every sub must have exactly one owner (DREAM or V2-fallback), confirm none falls through both; the 11 re-shared + 2 multi-target-break loops emit faithful `goto L_x` (expected).
>
> **BUILD LADDER (each rung lands gate-green + measured on the corpus, like V2's ladder):**
>   1. ~~**Condition-based refinement ŌåÆ nested if/else**~~ **Ō£ģ DONE 2026-06-08** (consensus simplifier + empty-then/arm-order flips + pre-pivot trunk). Plus the AST-native gate (the original "address-anchored" assumption replaced ŌĆö DREAM's whole point realized).
>   2. **Condition-AWARE refinement** ŌåÉ NEXT ŌĆö detect the genuine merge point so a multi-path block (reached under a disjunction) emits ONCE instead of re-guarded; + value-diamond pre-contraction (`$D2A2`). THEN **condition-aware switch** (`$D5`/`$D9`; cf. V2's atom-4 in [[decompiler-atom-log]]).
>   3. **Loop inference** ŌĆö the paper's loop-structuring rules (natural loops + `continue`/`break` from the condition formulas); reuse `vm_cfg.natural_loop`/`back_edges`.
>   4. **Semantics-preserving transforms for irreducibles** ŌĆö the paper's transforms that restructure genuinely-improper regions instead of emitting a goto (where V2 keeps an honest goto). This is DREAM's structural answer to V2's `_flat_span`/honest-goto residue.
>   5. **Stronger simplifier** ŌĆö condition formulas grow; the boolean simplifier needs to keep emitted predicates readable (this is where DREAM either wins or loses on readability vs V2).
>   6. ~~**Bake-off + cutover decision**~~ **Ō£ģ DONE 2026-06-10 ŌĆö DREAM WINS; verdict = displace V2 as PRIMARY, retain V2 as FALLBACK for a 24-sub hard tail.** Full-corpus head-to-head (495 subs, banks 0/1/2/15): **goto-free subs DREAM 471/495 (95.2%) vs V2 384/495 (77.6%)** (+87); total gotos V1 1072 / V2 827 / **DREAM 0** over its 471; **DREAM strict-wins 88 subs** (erasing 513 V2 gotos), **strict-loses exactly 1** (`$A45A`), and its 24-sub hard tail ŌŖé V2's (23/24 V2 also can't clear, often far worse). All gates green both sides. Corpus-count correction: the old "343/360" omitted bank 15 ŌĆö true number is 471/495. The two OPTIONAL levers that shrink the V2-fallback set ŌåÆ full cutover (kept alive, not dropped): **idiomatic-goto re-sharing** (folds the 7 over-dups) and **hard-tail loops** (the 16 passthrough). Wiring the DREAM-canonical generator (DREAM-emit + V2 fallback ŌåÆ `decompiled/*.c`) is the follow-on execution step. Full data + decision: [[decompiler-dream-thesis]] build log.
>
> **VALIDATION (unchanged safety model):** the existing CFG-equivalence gate proves **correctness** (propose an AST ŌåÆ gate proves CFG-equivalence or rejects); the **`--raw` witness** proves the round-trip; the **[[lowering-atlas]]** is the **readability** ground-truth oracle (and compiler-independence is what makes that oracle transfer cleanly). No new verification machinery ŌĆö DREAM plugs into the same gate V2 uses.
>
> **DETAILED THESIS + WORKED EXAMPLES:** [[decompiler-dream-thesis]] (`decompiler-dream-thesis.md`) ŌĆö the method writeup, the V2-vs-DREAM contrast in depth, and the running build log. (This ROADMAP entry is the index; the thesis page is where the per-rung work is recorded.)

### EPIC: CONTROL-FLOW STRUCTURING (V2 region reducer) ŌĆö goto ŌåÆ readable C (Chris, 2026-06-03; REFRAMED ŌåÆ REGION REDUCER 2026-06-04)
> **Ō¢Č SIBLING:** the [[decompiler-dream-thesis]] DREAM structurer (EPIC above) is the NEW parallel approach ŌĆö same readable-C goal, pattern-INDEPENDENT method. V2 (this epic) remains canonical/default until DREAM proves Ōēź it through the gate.
> **Ō¢ČŌ¢ČŌ¢Č RECALIBRATION DUE (2026-06-05) ŌĆö stop grinding atoms, run a divergent tournament.** Atoms 6ŌåÆ7ŌåÆ8 landed (V2 980ŌåÆ929, ŌłÆ51); the **forward-slice majority is harvested**. The residue (51 subs / 208 gotos behind V1) is dominated by ONE recurring wall: **the gate validates by ADDRESS ORDER** ŌĆö "address-ordered/based/inverted" appears **49├Ś** in this log as the blocker (atom-4 switch, atom-5 terminal-dup, atom-6 inverted-sink, atom-8 backward merge, the `$AD38` family, the 130-goto "neither" bucket). And the trap: **every fix ever tried changes the EMITTER** (the atoms, "address-ordered emitter", "redirect predecessors") ŌĆö the gate's *equivalence relation* has never once been a candidate in ~200 sessions. So the **untried DUAL** is to make the gate **reorder-invariant** (compare CFGs up to block permutation), so backward merges + interleaved switches validate *as-is* with no emitter rearchitecture ŌĆö and it's *cheaper* than the emitter route.
> **THE MOVE:** prototype **B (reorder-invariant gate)** vs **C (address-reassigning emitter)** on the backward/switch residue; the gate judges the winner. This is *1 approach vs another*, NOT variations on if-node folding (the `_COMBOS` grid was variations ŌĆö it can't escape a wall baked into the theme). *(Surfaced by running the vault's Anchor Method recalibration check on this project; principle: to invert something, learn the forward mechanism and invert THAT ŌĆö output-clues are a confession you haven't learned it. Consider reading GCC's actual CFG-construction passes as the deductive rival to the empirical atom-hunt.)*
> **Ō£ģ B TESTED + LANDED 2026-06-05 ŌĆö the bet is HALF-RIGHT: B enables, C exploits; NOT alternatives.** Made the gate reorder-invariant for the if/else MERGE: `vm_cfg.lower_struct_cfg` now reads the merge LEXICALLY by its LABEL (`merge_after`), not by `next_leader` (address). PROVABLY sound ŌĆö label-resolution IS the true C semantics (a join is always labelled; a backward merge ALWAYS is, since you can't fall backward), so it only removes false rejects (114/114 incl. negative misroute tests; hard gate 495/495 + 495/495; witness untouched; deterministic). **Result: V1 templates 1151 ŌåÆ 1080 (ŌłÆ71 gotos, fallbacks 35 ŌåÆ 15); `decompiled/*.c` regenerated with real structure recovered. V2 reducer 929 ŌåÆ 929 (INERT).** So the gate WAS a genuine wall ŌĆö but only the V1 emitter (which produces backward/flat-text merges) benefits; the V2 reducer doesn't GENERATE backward-merge candidates, so a gate-only change can't help it. Root cause pinned: behind-V1 subs route to the region-fallback, whose `_REGION_COMBOS` disables `merge_nonadj` (atom-8 greedy seam); naively re-enabling regressed V2 929ŌåÆ931. **Ō¢Č CHASE-V2 ATTEMPT ŌĆö the GLOBAL region assignment (atom-8 deferred) is PROVEN INERT, reverted.** Built it: coordinate-descent global region assignment (monotonic from flat, can't regress) + full `_COMBOS` grid (merge_nonadj on) in the fallback, ranked by the exact peephole-aware gate. Result: **V2 929ŌåÆ929, byte-identical** ŌĆö with the gate reorder-invariant AND the reducer free to use merge_nonadj globally, V2 gains nothing. So **the gate was NOT V2's wall.** atom-8 already harvested the forward non-adjacent merges; the residue is **shape-specific**, not backward-merges: goto-into-block short-circuit `||` (`$9A5D`, likely a missed `boolean_regions` shape), rotated-for-with-increment-in-`else` (`$9C22`), and the switch shared-merge (atom 4). **Ō¢ČŌ¢Č NEXT V2 lever = one of THOSE atoms** (start with the `||` goto-into-block as a `boolean_regions` extension, or atom-4 switch) ŌĆö the merge/gate/region-assignment lane is exhausted. Full diagnosis: [[decompiler-atom-log]] ┬¦"GATE CHANGE" + "CHASE-V2 ATTEMPT". So the recalibration's "B *instead of* C, cheaper" framing is corrected to: B is a cheap+sound win for the V1 emitter, but it does NOT move the V2 cutover target ŌĆö that needs shape-specific atoms.
>
> **Ō£ģ ATOM 9 ŌĆö CONTROL SHORT-CIRCUIT `if(c1||c2ŌĆ”){body}` ŌĆö LANDED 2026-06-05 (the first ATLAS-SOURCED atom; method validated).** The reframe Chris pushed (measurement is wrong; use the FORWARD source of truth to fix ARCHITECTURE, not chase gotos) ŌĆö TESTED on real code and it WORKS. Took `$9A5D`'s goto-into-block residue to the [[lowering-atlas]]: GCC's `b_or` proves `if(a||b){ŌĆ”}` lowers to exactly that shape (body reached from both guard-true edges) ŌĆö a REAL lowering, not irreducibility. The architecture gap it named: `boolean_regions` inverts only the VALUE diamond (`cond?a:b`); a CONTROL `||` had no inverse ŌåÆ the body's 2nd entry edge reads as a cross-edge and the reducer bails. Built `vm_cfg.control_shortcircuits` (detector) + `bytecode_cfg` contraction + a decoder fold (capture each guard's cond, emit ONE compound `if(!(c1||c2ŌĆ”)) goto skip`, the if-then structurer folds it) ŌĆö same pre-contraction playbook as value-diamonds, NO new reducer rule. **Result: V2 929 ŌåÆ 899 (ŌłÆ30, 13 subs, 0 worse), V1 1080 ŌåÆ 1038 (ŌłÆ42), raw 2032; all gates green** (witness 495/495, structuring 495/495, soundness 114/114, drift clean, disasm 0 BAD, deterministic; `decompiled/*.c` regenerated ŌĆö `$9A5D` reads `if((local11||local10)){ŌĆ”}`). **Two gate-INVISIBLE soundness traps caught (the recurring lesson):** (1) a non-entry guard with a side effect / call-valued cond would be hoisted to run unconditionally ŌåÆ detector requires non-entry guards side-effect-free; (2) the first cut broke the WITNESS (`lower(raw)==bytecode`) on 19 subs by assuming the body is the fall-through ŌåÆ fixed by requiring the tail fall into the body + address-contiguous chain. **The discovery sub `$9A5D` itself barely moved in V2 (13ŌåÆ12) ŌĆö the ŌłÆ30 is almost all OTHER subs: the atom folds BEYOND its purpose (Chris's "real, not chasing" bar ŌĆö MET).** Full writeup: [[decompiler-atom-log]] ┬¦"Atom 9". **Ō¢ČŌ¢Č NEXT atoms (now clearly atlas-sourceable): mixed `(a&&b)||c` (a guard not branching straight to body), then atom-4 switch shared-merge.**
>
> **Ō£ģ ATOM 4 (FIRST SHAPE) ŌĆö SWITCH empty-default==merge ŌĆö LANDED 2026-06-05 (Chris's target, `$A30D`).** The long-deferred switch mini-epic, attacked on `per_period_fief_daimyo_update_driver $A30D`. Atlas-confirmed forward (`06_switch_shared_merge.sm_default_preswitch_share`: `switch{ŌĆ”default:break;}` ŌåÆ each case ŌåÆ merge, empty default ŌåÆ merge). **A correctness catch on the way:** Chris's desired `case 0:ŌĆ”break;` looked like it might drop a fall-through (the TEXT shows `L_A37E`/`L_A385` adjacent) ŌĆö but the bytecode (`A37EŌåÆ{A381}`) proved case 0 jumps to the MERGE, not case 1 (the adjacency is the flushed-call display artifact); **case-0 break is correct.** Also pinned the readability gap: V1 "folds" this switch gate-equivalently but emits `case 0: default: L_A381: per_turn_age(); ŌĆ”` which READS as "default runs per_turn_age" (false) ŌĆö the gate-equivalent-yet-mis-reading case a single metric misses. **Fix (3 coordinated):** (1) `switch_dispatches` detects `default_is_merge` + sets `break_target=M` even when M is interleaved by address; (2) `_structure_switch` pulls M out, converts each case's `goto M`/fall-to-M ŌåÆ `break;`, omits the empty default, resumes at M; (3) **gate keystone** ŌĆö `lower_struct` now models `break` inside a switch (split `break_exit` [innermost loop OR switch] vs `continue_hdr` [innermost loop]) + an inlined no-default switch's fall = the LEXICAL merge. **Result: `$A30D` 8ŌåÆ0 (the EXACT clean break form, reads as game logic); V2 899 ŌåÆ 883 (ŌłÆ16, 4 subs, 0 worse); V1 unchanged (`decompiled/*.c` byte-identical)**; all gates green (witness 495/495, soundness 114/114, drift clean, deterministic). The switch-`break` gate model is the REUSABLE keystone for the remaining switch shapes (shared-return `$9C84`, non-empty default). Full writeup: [[decompiler-atom-log]] ┬¦"Atom 4 (FIRST SHAPE)".
>
> **Ō¢ČŌ¢Č NEXT LEVER (2026-06-05, data-grounded) ŌĆö the EMIT-ORDER GATE (lexical fall-through).** `probe-residue-cause.py` over the 56 behind-V1 subs: **63% (39 subs / 141 gotos) is the "neither" bucket = address-inverted LAYOUT**, plus the blocked atom 5 (terminal-dup, 11 subs / Ōēż56). All ONE capability gap: `lower_struct`'s fall-through is address-based (`next_leader[L]`), so a CORRECT structuring emitted out of address order is rejected. atom B fixed this for if-MERGES (label-anchored `merge_after`); the general fall-through is the lever ŌĆö the hard part is a fall-reached block has NO label to anchor on. A broad atlas-vs-V2 walk is LOWER value now (the shapes are known; the gap is layout-handling, not missing inverse-lowerings). **The method, the lessons (push/pull + atlas grounding + the gate-equivalentŌēĀreads-right / negative-tests-as-backstop / don't-land-inert findings), and a dedicated WORKED-EXAMPLES section for this problem are in [[decompiler-method]]** ŌĆö `$AD38` dissected, `$8172`/`$9A5D`/`$A2D2`/`$B89B` teed up, 3 candidate approaches (lead: the reducer emits a label on a reordered fall target so the gate anchors on it like `merge_after`). Recommended entry = approach B on `$AD38`'s `AD7BŌåÆAD67` (lands atom 5 + starts the 141-goto majority with one mechanism).
>
> **PURPOSE (the why ŌĆö [[project_nobunaga_decompiler_purpose]]):** convert the codebase into the LLM's *reliable* modality (READING code) so Pass-2 can re-walk the mechanics by reading, not by "put it in a machine and find out what happened." **DONE = the C reads as game logic, NOT goto-countŌåÆ0.** Honest gotos in genuinely-irreducible regions are CORRECT (Ghidra/Hex-Rays do the same).
> **THE REFRAME (Chris, 2026-06-04):** the gotos are **assembly leftovers from a structured-C source the compiler flattened** ŌĆö the job is to RECOVER the structure the compiler erased, not to delete gotos (goto-count is a symptom; structure is the thing). This is squarely **Pass-2 / validate-the-VM**, and it should have been an EARLY step ŌĆö the template-matching detour was the tax for not building the reducer first.
>
> **Ōøö THE TEMPLATE APPROACH IS RETIRED (decision 2026-06-04).** Phases 0ŌĆō3 (the superseded detail below) built a per-shape pattern matcher (`structure_lines` Pattern A/B/short-circuit + `structure_loops` while/do-while/while1/siblings + `structure_switches`). It WORKS and folded the high-value structural shapes (88 loops + 18 switches; 1437ŌåÆ1151 gotos) ŌĆö but it **structurally cannot converge**: template-matching has no *closure under composition*, so every new combination (e.g. a short-circuit `&&` feeding an if/else with a join ŌĆö `draw_daimyo_portrait` $E76F renders 4 gotos for what is one `if/else`) looks like a brand-new shape and spawns a new sub-step. **That is the "the stack never collapses" pathology** Chris flagged 2026-06-04. Kept below as history + as the fallback structurer until V2 dominates.
>
> **Ō¢ČŌ¢Č THE ONE OPEN FRAME ŌĆö REGION REDUCER (structural analysis / "No More Gotos").** Replace the menagerie with a single bottom-up CFG reducer:
>   - **Input = the basic-block CFG** (`vm_cfg.bytecode_cfg`), NOT line-text (the flat-text assumption is the source of every hoist/relocation bug in the templates). Leaves carry the C statements the expression layer already emits.
>   - **~7 fixed rules** ŌĆö `sequence ┬Ę if-then ┬Ę if-then-else ┬Ę short-circuit(&&/||) ┬Ę while ┬Ę do-while ┬Ę switch` ŌĆö applied to a **FIXPOINT**. Each firing collapses its subgraph into ONE abstract node consumed *identically to a basic block* ŌåÆ **closed under composition** ŌåÆ infinite combinations from a fixed grammar (the exact property the templates lack). This is RE-as-parsing: code-gen walks DOWN the grammar, the reducer builds UP the same grammar [[feedback_re_is_multipass_compilation]].
>   - **Irreducible residue** (a goto INTO a block / multi-entry) ŌåÆ break one edge with an honest goto, continue. Few, because most of the 1151 are reducible.
>   - **Reuses the expensive half UNCHANGED:** the CFG-equivalence gate (`structured_equivalent` + the `--raw` witness) is the reducer's verifier ŌĆö propose an AST, the gate proves CFG-equivalence or REJECTS. Same safety model, zero new verification work ŌĆö the hard, valuable half is already built.
>   - **Net code DELETION** ŌĆö retires Pattern A/B + all of `structure_loops` + `structure_switches` for ~7 rules + 1 fallback [[feedback_high_quality_code_not_more_code]].
>   - **Safe cutover:** build behind a `STRUCTURE_V2` flag, run it through the SAME gate, diff its output vs the current canonical `*.c`; land it only when it folds Ōēź the templates with every gate green; **delete the templates LAST.** Nested loops + the disguised-if/else cases fall out for FREE ŌĆö they stop being separate tickets.
>   - **TEST CORPUS = the already-discovered gotos (Chris, 2026-06-04: "test it on the discovered gotos to verify it works").** The subs the templates already fold (88 loops + 18 switches + the diamonds/boolean regions) are V2's **regression oracle** ŌĆö V2 must structure them Ōēź as well, every fold gate-green; the current goto residue (35 fallbacks) + the disguised-`if/else` (`$E76F draw_daimyo_portrait`) are its **new-win targets**. Build V2 against this corpus incrementally, one rule at a time, gate-green each step.
>   - **DoD ŌĆö the epic RETURNS here:** V2 is the sole structurer; all gates green (cfg 495/495 witness + 495/495 gated, round-trip 495/45024, drift CLEAN, `--check` 0 BAD ├Ś4); remaining gotos are *only* genuinely-irreducible regions; `decompiled/*.c` regenerated + a spot-read confirms subs read as game logic; templates deleted.
>   - **BUILD LADDER (Chris's call 2026-06-04: persist + start a FRESH task-scoped session ŌĆö this is its plan).** Integration is one surgical swap: V2 lives behind a `STRUCTURE_V2` flag and replaces the three `structure_*` calls at `vm_decompile.py:1204-1206`, feeding the **UNCHANGED** `structured_equivalent` gate (consumes `(addr,indent,text)` line lists, so V2 must emit the same line format). **New code = a region-tree builder over `vm_cfg.bytecode_cfg` + a treeŌåÆlines pretty-printer; the leaves (`state.lines`), the verifier (`structured_equivalent`), and the detectors (`boolean_regions`/`value_diamonds`/`switch_dispatches`/`natural_loop`/`back_edges`/`dominators`/`post_dominators`) ALL already exist in `vm_cfg.py`.** Each rung lands gate-green + measured on the corpus:
>     0. **Harness + passthrough ŌĆö Ō£ģ DONE 2026-06-04.** `tools/vm_reduce.py` (the reducer's home; rung-0 `reduce()` = passthrough returning the raw lines + the full build-ladder docstring), `vm_decompile.STRUCTURE_V2` flag (default OFF) + `structure_v2()` delegate, and the `decompile()` gate-wiring split into a self-contained V2 branch (one-pass full-or-honest-goto gate) vs the untouched V1 template branch (`elif`). `tools/v2-corpus.py` = THE regression oracle, wired first: runs all 495 subs through BOTH structurers, categorises V2 (folded/honest-goto/gate-reject), and reports the **BEHIND-V1 work-list** (subs where V2 leaves more gotos than templates ŌåÆ target 0). **Rung-0 numbers:** V2 passthrough = 495 honest-goto / 0 folded / 0 reject; goto totals raw **2068** ŌåÆ V1(templates) **1151** ŌåÆ V2 **2068**; **296 subs behind V1** = the ladder work-list. Gates green BOTH ways: default path (`STRUCTURE_V2=False`) `decompiled/*.c` **byte-identical**, V1 cfg-gate 495/495 + 495/495 (34 fallbacks = baseline); V2 path (`STRUCTURE_V2=True`) cfg-gate **495/495 + 495/495, 0 fallbacks** (passthrough is trivially CFG-faithful = raw). The harness + gate + oracle are proven BEFORE any reduction rule can introduce a bug.
>     1. **Block model + trivial emit ŌĆö Ō£ģ DONE 2026-06-04.** `vm_reduce._partition` groups the raw leaves into `{leader: [(addr,indent,text)ŌĆ”]}` by `block_of(addr)` (preserving each line's list order within its block), and `reduce()` emits the buckets in leader (address) order. **Faithfulness PROVEN across all 495:** the line MULTISET is unchanged (0 subs add/drop/alter a line) and every block's WITHIN-block order is byte-identical to raw (0 within-block reorders). The only difference from raw is **block-order normalization on 105 subs** ŌĆö the decompiler's flushed-call artifact (a discarded side-effecting CALL is printed at its later flush point but tagged with its earlier call-site addr, so raw prints e.g. `ui_helper_d759()` $8096 *after* the label `L_8099:` though it executes first; per-block emit restores true address/execution order). All 105 are gate-certified CFG-equivalent. V2 cfg-gate **495/495 + 495/495, 0 fallbacks**; default path byte-identical. So the blockŌåöline round-trip is faithful at the block granularity the gate validates ŌĆö the foundation rungs 2-6 build the region tree on.
>     2. **`sequence` + `if-then` + `if-then-else` ŌĆö Ō£ģ DONE 2026-06-04.** `vm_reduce._structure` recursively structures the single-entry region of an ACYCLIC sub (entryŌåÆEXIT) into a Seq/IfThen/IfElse tree, using the immediate post-dominator as each 2-way branch's merge; `_emit` pretty-prints it. Branch polarity mirrors the decompiler exactly (raw `if (RAWC) goto L_T` ŌåÆ then-body = the FALL-THROUGH arm, cond = `_neg(RAWC)`, and `simplify_expression` cleans `!((a<b))`ŌåÆ`(a>=b)`). **Result: 112 subs folded, gotos 2068ŌåÆ1845, 0 gate-rejects** (all fallback decisions STRUCTURAL ŌĆö the gate stays a pure backstop, never the control mechanism). Loops (back edge present) and switches bail to the rung-1 flat emit (rungs 4/5). **Two soundness guards earned their keep against real rejects** (the gate caught them; I converted each to a structural rule so they bail to flat, not gate-reject): (1) **merge lexical-adjacency** ŌĆö `next_leader(max consumed) == merge`, else an outer arm laid out between a construct and its shared merge interleaves (`$8F0A`, twin nested if/else sharing one merge); (2) **arm address-disjointness** ŌĆö `max(then_used) < min(else_used)`, else emitting then-then-else reverses address order and the address-based gate mis-routes (`$A853`, a nested if whose arm sits at a higher addr than the outer else-body). Both are the invariant *lexical order == address order* that the gate (and readable C) rely on. **Faithfulness PROVEN over all 495:** the NON-scaffold statement multiset is unchanged (0 subs alter a real statement ŌĆö only `if`/braces/`goto`/labels change). Gate green: V2 cfg-gate **495/495 + 495/495, 0 fallbacks**; default path byte-identical. (Pre-existing cosmetic noise inherited from V1, NOT a regression: empty `if(c){}else{}` diamonds from un-contracted value-diamonds ŌĆö e.g. `read_frame_timer` $D29D, where V2 actually folds the surrounding gotos V1 left.)
>     3. **`short-circuit (&&/||)`** ŌĆö reuse `boolean_regions`/`recover_bool_formula`. Target = the disguised-if/else (`$E76F draw_daimyo_portrait`, `is_tile_in_bounds`).
>     4. **`while` / `do-while` / `while(1)` ŌĆö Ō£ģ DONE 2026-06-04.** `vm_reduce._structure_loop` collapses each natural loop (`back_edges`/`natural_loop`) to ONE `('loop',ŌĆ”)` AST node the surrounding walk consumes like a basic block, so rung-2 if/then/else composes inside AND around loops (the closure payoff ŌĆö no `_emit_break_continue` gymnastics). Form read from the CFG: pre-test `while(C)` (header is the 2-way exit test; rotated for-loops lift ONLY the test expr, the update keeps its addr at the body bottom), post-test `do{}while(C)` (a single latch's 2-way test), `while(1)` (exits via break/return). Inside a body, an edge to the header = `continue`, to the exit = `break`, a bare-return target = an INLINED `return X;` (early-return idiom; kills the shared-return-tail cross-edge that blocked acyclic subs too); in-body merges use a body-LOCAL post-dominator (drop loop-leaving edges + sink-fill, so a breaking arm doesn't pull the merge to EXIT). **Result: 171 subs fold (112ŌåÆ171), gotos 1845ŌåÆ1624 (raw 2068), behind-V1 197ŌåÆ142, 0 gate-rejects** (the reducer is SOUND ŌĆö every emitted fold passes the gate). All fallbacks are STRUCTURAL bails earned against real gate-rejects (57ŌåÆ0 during the build): nested loops (4d), compound multi-exit-test loops (`while(a&&b)`, need rung 3), a loop whose exit is non-adjacent or a pure-routing/invisible block (loop-as-tail-of-if-arm), an empty then-arm hiding a goto-side body. V2 cfg-gate **495/495 + 495/495, 0 fallbacks**; default `*.c` byte-identical (`vm-cfg-gate.py --v2` added to validate the V2 path). Remaining 142-behind = 97 loops (4d/rung-3), 32 acyclic (rung 3 short-circuit), 13 switch (rung 5).
>     5. **`switch`** ŌĆö reuse `switch_dispatches`. Target = the 18 switches + the 7 nested-in-`if`/`while` residue (the tree nests natively, so they fall out for free).
>     6. **Irreducible local fallback ŌĆö Ō£ģ LARGELY DONE 2026-06-04 (session 6).** The convergence move: when the clean recovery raises on a shape it can't own, DON'T flatten the whole sub ŌĆö keep that ONE edge as an honest goto and structure everything around it. Landed incrementally, every step gate-green + sound (0 gate-rejects throughout; the gate stays a pure backstop, never the control mechanism): **(a) self-loop do-while fix** ŌĆö a self-loop (header==latch) was mis-detected as a pre-test while, walking into its own visited header ŌåÆ spurious cross_edge (cross_edge ŌłÆ13 subs). **(b) bare self-loop fold/keep** ŌĆö `loop=={h}`: while(1){stmts} when it carries statements, else an honest `goto self`; new `_insert_labels` post-pass restores `L_xxxx:` for any kept honest goto (clean folds emit none ŌåÆ no-op). **(c) the if/else honest-goto fallback** ŌĆö the big one: a 2-way branch the structurer can't own (shared continuation = cross_edge, non-adjacent merge, goto-past-merge, empty-then, reversed arms) is kept as `if (rawcond) goto L_t;` verbatim (CFG-faithful by construction) and the walk continues at fall. SOUNDNESS GUARD: only when goto_block is reachable FROM fall (else it would orphan the target ŌåÆ re-raise, whole-sub bails). **(d) rung 4d nested loops** compose for free (drop the blanket inner-header bail) with two precise structural guards: multi-latch inner, and inner-while-ending-a-do-while-body whose exit is the enclosing do-while's EMPTY latch (renders as `} while` scaffold the gate can't anchor ŌåÆ bail). **(e) multi-exit loops via early-return exits** ŌĆö an exit to a bare-return block is an early return (inlined by `_terminal`), not a competing exit; drop those from the count (and in the all-return search-loop case, the header's own non-body successor is the natural exit). **(f) pure-routing exit at top level** ŌĆö only bail it inside a BOUNDED region (if-arm / loop body, where the gate scans past the boundary); at the sub's top level contract() absorbs it. **Session 6 net: behind-V1 127ŌåÆ82, folded 287ŌåÆ311, V2 gotos ~1498ŌåÆ1264, 0 gate-rejects, hard gate 495/495+495/495 both paths, default `*.c` byte-identical.** Remaining 82-behind = genuine multi-exit loops needing break-via-goto (19), cross-edges in loop bodies (18), un-foldable switches (9), goto-past-merge (4), compound pre-tests (6), a few merge/exit-adjacency tails. `$9A0F` fully-rotated loop is ACCEPTED residue (honest goto).
>     7. **Cutover** ŌĆö V2 folds Ōēź templates across all 495, every gate green ŌåÆ flip the default on, regen `decompiled/*.c`, spot-read, DELETE `structure_loops`/`structure_lines`/`structure_switches` + dead helpers. Epic RETURNS.
>     **Ō¢Č AUDIT of the 82 behind-V1 (2026-06-04, "audit first" before writing more reducer code ŌĆö Chris's call).** Verdict: **0 of 82 are genuinely-irreducible residue to accept ŌĆö the cutover bar (behind-V1 == 0) STANDS, relax nothing.** Measured via `v2-corpus.py --behind`, classifying each by V2-gotos vs raw-gotos: **81 of 82 are WHOLE-SUB BAILS** (V2_gotos == raw_gotos ŌĆö V2 gives up structuring the ENTIRE sub over ONE unhandled local shape, discarding the cleanly-reducible loops/branches around it). Canonical example `$A30D` (season-turn): two counted `while` loops + a `switch(current_season)`, all trivially reducible, emitted **100% flat** because the switch's shared-tail cross-edge raised `_NotReducible`. Only `$9F04` is a true partial (V2 1 / V1 0). **ROOT CAUSE: rung-6 local containment is implemented for ONLY the if/then/else 2-way-branch bail** (the `try/except _NotReducible` at `vm_reduce.py:359-441`). Bails from `_structure_loop` (multi_exit_loop / nested_loop / exit_not_adjacent / exit_is_dowhile_latch / compound_pretest, called unguarded at `:299-305`), the linear-strand `cross_edge` raise (`:314`), `multiway` (`:443`), and the `switch_unfoldable` pre-check (`:734`) ALL propagate uncaught to `reduce()`'s top `except` (`:748-750`) ŌåÆ whole-sub `_flat_emit`. **THE FIX is ONE structural property, not 12 separate rules:** generalize the if/else local fallback into a `_flat_span` ŌĆö when any rule can't own a region (loop / switch / linear strand), keep THAT region as an honest-goto span and continue structuring around it. Recovers most of the 346 recoverable gotos across ALL bail reasons at once. Lands as a few SOUND increments (the gate anchors by address, so a flat span must stay address-contiguous and the continuation must anchor on the address-next block ŌĆö the same soundness pattern the existing `ifgoto` fallback's `_reaches` guard already proves), biggest-lever first: cross_edge (97 gotos / 18 subs) ŌåÆ multi_exit_loop (77 / 19) ŌåÆ switch_unfoldable (50 / 9). **This finishes rung 6 (local containment was always its thesis); it is NOT a new open frame.**
>     **Ō¢Č SESSION 7a ŌĆö cross_edge bucket attacked (2026-06-04). behind-V1 82ŌåÆ77, V2 gotos 1264ŌåÆ1242, folded 311ŌåÆ314, gate-green BOTH paths (V2 495/495+495/495 0-fallback; V1 default byte-identical; drift clean).** Attacking cross_edge surfaced THREE bugs the whole-sub bail had masked (instrumented the raise site ŌåÆ split `cross_edge` into `cross_edge_top` [merge/after re-entry] vs `cross_edge_fall` [single-succ fall-into-visited]): **(1)** the `while(1)` endless path pre-marked the header visited then walked the body FROM it ŌåÆ instant spurious `cross_edge_top` on its own header (every multi-latch/endless loop bailed); fixed by dropping the pre-add (`_terminal` already maps edges-to-h as `continue`). **(2)** a MULTI-LATCH loop has no sound single-construct form (a `while(1)` body-tail `if(C) continue;` exits via fall, but the gate reads that fall as the back-edge and loses the exit) ŌĆö built the audit's **`_flat_span`** (keep the loop's RAW lines as an honest-goto region, structure everything around it, exactly as V1 leaves them) and routed multi-latch loops to it. **(3)** pre-test fired BEFORE do-while for a loop matching BOTH shapes, rendering an unsound body-tail break; fixed by computing `clean_dowhile` (single 2-way exit-testing latch) and gating pre-test off it (a 1-way for-update latch doesn't divert, so for-loops are unaffected). Canonical win `$88AC` (4 stacked loops incl. one multi-latch): whole-bail 6 gotos ŌåÆ folds to **2, matching V1** (multi-latch as honest gotos + a do-while + two do-whiles). Remaining cross_edge: `cross_edge_top` 4 subs/55g (big improper regions), `cross_edge_fall` 10/32 (single-succ cut regresses inside if/else arm probes ŌĆö needs the cut confined to committed strands). **NEXT lever by gain: multi_exit_loop (21/80) ŌĆö `_flat_span` likely generalizes straight to it.**
>     **Ō¢Č SESSION 7b ŌĆö multi_exit_loop CONVERGENT-EXIT (2026-06-04). behind-V1 77ŌåÆ75, V2 gotos 1242ŌåÆ1205 (ŌłÆ37), bank 2 reaches V1 PARITY (401=401), gate-green both paths (V2 0-fallback, V1 byte-identical, drift clean).** Most "multi-exit" loops aren't really multi-exit ŌĆö their N immediate exit targets CONVERGE on one block (the others are loop-private "exit shims" that flow to it). New `_convergent_exit`: pick the convergence block `c` as the single exit and let the shims be walked as in-body break paths (shim-aware `region = loop | shims` drives the exit-adjacency check + consumed accounting). `c` may be a target itself (`$8C45`'s `8C6D`, reached directly + via the `local11=1` shim `8C61`) or a common successor of all targets (`$ADF6`'s `AE77`). Canonical win `$8C45`: whole-bail 5 gotos ŌåÆ **0, BEATING V1's 1** (`while(local10){ ŌĆ”; if(ai_state){ local11=1; break; } local10--; }`). multi_exit_loop 21ŌåÆ17 subs. >     **Ō¢Č SESSION 7c ŌĆö switch_unfoldable LOCALIZED + orphan self-check (2026-06-04). behind-V1 75ŌåÆ74, V2 gotos 1205ŌåÆ1200, folded 316ŌåÆ321, bank 2 drops BELOW V1 (398<401), gate-green both paths (0-fallback / byte-identical / drift clean).** The old whole-sub `switch_unfoldable` pre-check is replaced by LOCAL handling inside `_structure`: an un-foldable switch dispatch is kept as an honest flat span of its whole TERRITORY (the dispatch + every case body reachable up to its post-dominator merge ŌĆö NOT just the dispatch block, or the goto-only case bodies orphan), continuing the walk at the merge so the code AROUND the switch still folds. Guarded to span the whole forward cone (no continuation) when the merge wraps mid-territory or is a shared continuation with external preds (else the address-based gate mis-routes ŌĆö `$D14E`). `switch_unfoldable` (9 subs/50g) is GONE from the bail histogram ŌĆö 8 fold/improve; the bucket is cleared. **Plus a GENERAL `orphan` STRUCTURAL self-check in `reduce()`:** a sound structuring preserves every real statement (assignment/call/return ŌĆö content the folds emit verbatim, vs scaffolding they rewrite); if a content stmt vanished, a block was orphaned ŌåÆ bail to flat BEFORE the gate sees it, keeping the gate a pure backstop and the 0-reject invariant. This caught `$D14E` (two un-foldable switches sharing a continuation that feeds the still-unsolved cross-edge structurer ŌåÆ drops blocks); it bails cleanly as `orphan` (1 sub/11g) instead of gate-rejecting. **Session 7 net (a+b+c): behind-V1 82ŌåÆ74, V2 gotos 1264ŌåÆ1200 (ŌłÆ64), folded 311ŌåÆ321, 0 gate-rejects throughout. NEXT levers: exit_not_adjacent (23/66), multi_exit_loop (17/72, divergent/nested), cross_edge (15/93, the deferred improper-region structurer ŌĆö also unblocks `$D14E`).**
>     **Ō¢Č SESSION 7d ŌĆö cross-edge cut + REDUCER SELF-VALIDATION (2026-06-04). behind-V1 74ŌåÆ70, V2 gotos 1200ŌåÆ1139, folded 321ŌåÆ324 ŌĆö and V2's TOTAL gotos (1139) drop BELOW V1's (1151): the reducer now beats the templates in aggregate.** The cross-edge residue (a `goto` to a shared mid-function continuation ŌĆö `goto cleanup`/`done`, short-circuit-OR) has NO structured-operator equivalent (`break`/`return` already cover loop/fn exits), so the faithful handling KEEPS one honest goto and structures around it ŌĆö what V1 and Ghidra/Hex-Rays do. Landed: **(a)** a FORWARD-only cross-edge cut in the linear walk ŌĆö a single-succ fall into an already-emitted *later* block becomes `goto L_s` (forward never reverses lexical-vs-address order; backward bails). **(b)** relaxed the if/else honest-goto fallback's `_reaches` re-raise guard (it existed to prevent orphaning). **(c)** the keystone ŌĆö `reduce()` now SELF-VALIDATES its output against `structured_equivalent` (the CFG-equivalence gate) and reverts to flat on failure. This is the design's own safety model applied as the reducer's acceptance test: composed local fallbacks (honest-goto cuts / flat spans / convergent exits) can emit a CFG-divergent LAYOUT (lexicalŌēĀaddress order, orphaned continuation) that no bespoke structural guard caught ŌĆö rather than enumerate every hazard, PROVE equivalence or revert. Makes "0 gate-rejects downstream" AUTOMATIC and subsumes the ad-hoc orphan check. Simple shared-continuations now fold (ŌłÆ61 gotos this step); genuinely-improper layouts (`$8BEA`, where V1 only wins by physically nesting the goto-target inside a sibling's `else` ŌĆö flat-text trickery a region tree won't do) bail cleanly as `self_gate` (23 subs/106g ŌĆö the new top bucket, mostly genuinely-improper residue). **Session 7 net so far: behind 82ŌåÆ70, V2 gotos 1264ŌåÆ1139 (ŌłÆ125), folded 311ŌåÆ324, 0 rejects. V2 < V1 aggregate.**
>     **Ō¢Č SESSION 7e ŌĆö REGION-LEVEL PARTIAL FALLBACK (2026-06-04). folded 324ŌåÆ350 (+26 subs recover structure), V2 gotos 1133 (stays below V1 1151), behind 70ŌåÆ67, 0 rejects.** The keystone for the whole-bailers: previously ONE improper region (a cross-edge, a non-adjacent-exit loop, a divergent multi-exit) flattened the ENTIRE sub via the all-or-nothing self-gate. Now `reduce()`: (1) tries whole-sub structuring, self-validated; (2) on failure, DECOMPOSES the sub at its post-dominator SPINE (the immediate-post-dom chain entryŌåÆŌĆ”ŌåÆEXIT ŌĆö the blocks all paths cross) into single-entry/single-exit regions, structures each INDEPENDENTLY, and keeps a region structured only if (it structured + every other region flat) self-validates AND emits Ōēż the flat span's gotos (an honest-goto cut can turn a raw fall-through into an explicit goto, so over-aggressive structuring is rejected in favour of the leaner flat). Regions join linearly at the articulation points, so a divergence in one improper region no longer destroys the reducible regions around it ŌĆö every kept piece CFG-proven. Also converted the `exit_not_adjacent` / divergent-`multi_exit_loop` loop bails to loop-local flat-spans (the region-fallback's per-loop analogue). **Spot-read `$A30D` (season-turn): was 100% flat, now structures BOTH counted loops (drift-luck + natural-death sweeps) cleanly, keeping only the improper `switch(season)` as honest gotos ŌĆö reads as game logic, the epic's actual DoD.** Cost: region-recovery's O(regions) extra gate calls fire only for the ~70 failing subs; full regen stays ~2.4s. **Session 7 net: behind 82ŌåÆ67, V2 gotos 1264ŌåÆ1133 (ŌłÆ131), folded 311ŌåÆ350 (+39), 0 gate-rejects throughout, V2 < V1 aggregate.** Residual 67 behind are genuinely-improper (V1 wins only via flat-text goto-into-block trickery) or need bespoke loop-model work ŌĆö the case for reframing the cutover bar from "behind-V1==0" to "V2 Ōēż V1 aggregate + residue genuinely-irreducible" (already MET). Cosmetic polish open: drop redundant `goto L_next; L_next:` at region boundaries (CFG-neutral peephole, guard on next_leader).
>     **Ō¢Č SESSION 7f ŌĆö backward cuts + self_gate ROOT-CAUSE (2026-06-04). behind 67ŌåÆ66, V2 gotos 1133ŌåÆ1126, 0 rejects.** Allowed BACKWARD cross-edge honest-goto cuts (self-validation makes them safe ŌĆö a reversing cut self-gates, a holding one is kept; covers shared `return`-block continuations reached from a later block). Then DIAGNOSED the 22 reduce-level `self_gate` residue (the only subs that render WORSE than V1 ŌĆö whole-flat goto-soup): **they are genuinely IMPROPER regions.** Spine is trivial ([entry, EXIT]) because early returns make every block's post-dominator EXIT (region-recovery can't decompose them), and **14 of 22 are LOOPLESS pure-branch tangles** (`$AD38`: shared `return` block `$AD58` reached from a LATER block `$AD67`; `$A2D2`: a 42-goto switch+branch handler V1 folds to 19). V1 wins ONLY by emitting blocks in ADDRESS-LAYOUT order with gotos ŌĆö physically placing `$AD67` before `$AD7B` and jumping back INTO the then-arm ŌĆö flat-text trickery a control-flow-following region reducer structurally cannot do (confirmed: V2 builds the right-looking tree but the address-based gate rejects the backward continuation `$AD67`<`$AD7B`). **CONCLUSION: matching V1 on these needs an ADDRESS-ORDERED partial-structure emitter** (walk leaders by address; fold loops + address-forward if/else IN PLACE; honest-goto the improper edges) ŌĆö the Ghidra/Hex-Rays model for irreducible regions, a defined ~bounded build that partially re-derives `structure_lines` composably. Per the epic's PURPOSE these 22 ARE the "genuinely-irreducible residue ŌĆ” honest gotos are CORRECT" ŌĆö the only gap is V2 flat-spans the WHOLE sub (goto-soup) instead of structuring the reducible parts WITHIN the irreducible layout. **CUTOVER OPTIONS: (a) build the address-ordered emitter ŌåÆ the 22 get partial structure (read far better than flat, may still trail V1's goto-count) ŌåÆ cleanest; (b) reframe the bar (V2<V1 aggregate + residue genuinely-irreducible, already MET) and cut over now, the 22 rendering as honest-goto until (a) lands.** Session 7 net: behind 82ŌåÆ66, V2 gotos 1264ŌåÆ1126 (ŌłÆ138), folded 311ŌåÆ350, 0 gate-rejects throughout, V2 < V1 aggregate. 7 commits.
>
>     **Ō¢Č SESSION 7g ŌĆö disjoint-region dead-code fix + CFG-neutral peephole (2026-06-04). behind 66ŌåÆ59, V2 gotos 1126ŌåÆ1045 (ŌłÆ81), V2 folds-below-raw 277ŌåÆ289, 0 rejects, 114/114 reducer tests pass, default `*.c` byte-untouched.** Two SOUND emit-quality wins (both V2-path only, self-validated): **(a) DISJOINT-REGION FIX (ŌłÆ60).** The region-partial-fallback's post-dom SPINE decomposition was NOT producing a true partition: when the spine cut through a loop, a back-edge from a LATER spine point (the loop latch) re-collected the ENTIRE loop body into an earlier-overlapping region, whose `_flat_span` then re-emitted the whole body as UNREACHABLE DEAD-DUPLICATE code ŌĆö CFG-equivalent (so the gate passed it) but DOUBLING the goto count (`$9A18`: body emitted twice, 31 gotos ŌåÆ 16). Fix: each region now walls off EVERY OTHER spine point (`spine_walls - {Pi}`), not just its exit Pj ŌĆö spine points are articulation points so nothing legitimately between Pi and Pj is one, making the regions disjoint. **(b) CFG-NEUTRAL PEEPHOLE (ŌłÆ21).** `_peephole` drops a standalone `goto L_X;` whose IMMEDIATELY-following emitted line is `L_X:` (redundant goto-to-fall-through, the honest-goto-cut / flat-span join boundary's `goto L_next; L_next:`) + any now-dead label; wired into `_validates` and KEPT only if it still proves `structured_equivalent` (the gate is the backstop for the rare emit-orderŌēĀaddress-order divergence). **TRIED & REVERTED: loop-aware spine** (filter cut points strictly inside a loop's address span so a loop stays whole in one region) ŌĆö REGRESSED 1066ŌåÆ1080. Diagnosis: the `none` bucket is NOT clean-loops-cut-by-spine; those loop BODIES are genuinely improper (`$9A18`'s cursor cross-edges), so even a whole-loop region bails to flat ŌĆö coarsening just merged more into the flat bail. The real lever is EMIT QUALITY, confirming 7f's address-ordered-emitter conclusion. **Remaining 59-behind** = `none` 42 (non-adjacent ROUTING-block forwarding `L_997D: goto L_9976;` + SWITCH-case inlining `case N: goto L` vs V1's inlined bodies ŌĆö the address-ordered-emitter work, must redirect predecessors under the address-based gate, not just delete lines) + `self_gate` 17 (genuinely-improper, per 7f). **Cutover bar (V2<V1 aggregate) now met DECISIVELY: 1045 vs 1151 (ŌłÆ106).** Chris's call: commit these, defer cutover-vs-emitter to next session.
>     **Ō¢Č REFRAME ŌĆö THE RESIDUE IS A PHANTOM (2026-06-04). `tools/probe-cfg-reducibility.py` census: all 495 subs are FORMALLY REDUCIBLE, 0 irreducible; all 59 behind-V1 are reducible.** So 7f's "genuinely irreducible residue needing an address-ordered emitter" was WRONG ŌĆö an artifact of top-down post-dom decomposition manufacturing false irreducibility from shared continuations (N blocks ŌåÆ a shared `return`). A reducible CFG always has a goto-free structured form Ō¤╣ the 59 behind-V1 are 100% MISSING-ATOMS (un-written inverse-lowerings, e.g. branch-to-terminal ŌćÆ `if(!c) return;`), 0% irreducibility Ō¤╣ the engine is structured-source-shaped and a finite bottom-up atom table decompiles it FULLY (nothing to "accept as honest gotos"). The goto-count metric was measuring missing atoms the whole time, which is what drove the rung-6 spawl (top-down has no graceful local fallback, so one was hand-built per shape). **NEXT SESSION starts at [[decompiler-bottom-up-thesis]] (`decompiler-bottom-up-thesis.md`): an atom-extraction loop ŌĆö pick a behind sub, NAME the forward lowering it inverts (gate against 1-offs), add the inverse as a CFG PRE-CONTRACTION (same mechanism as the value-diamond pre-contraction ŌĆö bottom-up by composition), DELETE the rung-6 handler it obsoletes, re-run the census (a real atom clears SEVERAL subs, a 1-off clears one). Solve-in-place and the bottom-up refactor are the SAME activity done this way; you reach the refactor by attrition, net-negative on rules, no big-bang rewrite. PoC (compile Small-C/lcc, read the jump patterns) hands you the complete finite atom table; it's rule-sourcing, not the architecture decision.** First atoms by the cross-tab: branch-to-terminal guard (`shared-ret>0` cluster) + switch-case inline (`shared-ret=0` cluster); test cases `$9A5D` (minimal) / `$A2D2` (biggest, gap 23) / `$A221` (non-guard atom).
>     **Ō¢Č SESSION 8 ŌĆö ATOM LOOP STARTED FROM THE ENTRY FUNCTION `vm_bootstrap $A778` (2026-06-05). V2 gotos 1045ŌåÆ1025 (ŌłÆ20), 3 subs improved / 0 worse, 0 gate-rejects, hard gate 495/495, 114/114 reducer tests, deterministic, default `*.c` byte-identical.** Chris's call: drive the loop from the project SPINE, not the synthetic test cases. `vm_bootstrap` was a WHOLE-SUB bail for both V1 and V2 (14 gotos each) ŌĆö its real shape is a **triple-nested `while(1)`** (per-game ŌåÆ per-turn `$A785` ŌåÆ per-fief `$A806`) with a `&128` abort gate that `goto`s `DISPLAY $A843` from all three levels. Two genuine **atoms** (missing inverse-lowerings) fold it to **1 goto** (the abort, a multi-level break C can't express ŌĆö Ghidra/Hex-Rays keep it too):
>       1. **MULTI-LATCH `while(1)`-with-`continue`s** ŌĆö a loop with >1 back-edge is the inverse of the compiler lowering each `continue` to a jump-to-header. Replaced the blanket multi-latch `_flat_span` bail (+ the `nested_loop` rung-4d guard, now DELETED) with an ATTEMPT at `while(1)` (body edges to the header render `continue`, to the exit `break`), reduce()'s self-validation the backstop. The one unsound shape (body-TAIL `if(C) continue;` whose fall IS the loop-back, where the gate collapses the exit into the back-edge) is handled by the both-terminal walk collapsing it to a single `if(!C) break;`. Folds `$88AC render_boot_title_screens` 2ŌåÆ0 (the session-7a "4 stacked loops" example, now BEATS V1) + `$D59D` 5ŌåÆ0.
>       2. **MULTI-LEVEL break = honest goto** ŌĆö a loop exit that escapes the PARENT loop too (`far_by_loop`, computed in `_structure_loop` relative to `outer_loop`) is kept as an honest `goto L_t` inside the body (via `_terminal`) and DROPPED from the loop's exit set, so the remaining single-level exit makes the loop foldable. This is what lets `vm_bootstrap`'s 3-level `goto DISPLAY` fold: each inner loop keeps the goto; only the outermost loop that still CONTAINS `$A843` breaks to it. Also tightened the `exit_is_dowhile_latch` bail to fire ONLY for single-latch (do-while) parents (a multi-latch parent renders `while(1)`, where the latch is a normal `if(cond) continue;` block the gate anchors on fine).
>     **Verified empirically** (not just the hard gate's formal CFG-equivalence): ran the `$A78C..A7B0` region's real ROM bytecode through `nobunaga_vm` for all 3 input combos ŌĆö `resumeŌēĀ1` skips the whole block (no calls, ŌåÆ `$A7B0`); `resume==1 & flags&128` runs `call_bank_wrap` but SKIPS `call_bank10_entry` (ŌåÆ `$A7AD`); `resume==1 & !(flags&128)` runs BOTH ŌĆö matching the fold's `if(resume==1){ŌĆ”; if(!(flags&128)){call_bank10_entry();} planner();}` exactly. (This also resolved Chris's review catch: the raw text's `L_A7AD: call_bank10_entry()` is the **flushed-call display artifact** ŌĆö a void call tagged with its earlier call-site addr `$A7A9` but printed after the `$A7AD` label; the address column proves the `goto L_A7AD` SKIPS the call, it does not jump-to-next-line, and the block-model fold re-orders it correctly. His negative-logic intuition `if(!X){body}` is precisely the `_neg(rawcond)` inversion the reducer applies.) **The entry function ŌĆö the project spine ŌĆö now reads as the documented per-game/per-turn/per-fief loop nest.** Note vs the thesis's "pure CFG pre-contraction" framing: these two are LOOP-SHAPE atoms, so they live in the loop structurer (`_structure_loop`/`_terminal`), not as `bytecode_cfg` pre-contractions (which fit expression-layer atoms like value-diamonds) ŌĆö but the spirit holds (named the inverse-lowering, deleted the rung-6 bail it obsoletes, measured on the corpus). Remaining behind-59 unchanged (these atoms are rare shapes; the behind list is still `none` 41 + `self_gate` 18 = the address-ordered-emitter / switch-inline work). **RETURN:** the atom loop is live and proven on the spine; next pick is the `none`-bucket atoms (routing-block forwarding + switch-case inline).
>     **Ō¢Č SESSION 9 ŌĆö ATOM 3 (routing-block absorption) + the running ATOM LOG (2026-06-05). V2 gotos 1025ŌåÆ988 (ŌłÆ37), 7 subs improved / 0 worse, behind-V1 59ŌåÆ57, 0 gate-rejects, hard gate 495/495, 114/114, deterministic, default `*.c` byte-identical.** Chris's discipline: **fix as we go but LOG each case** to tell a real atom from a 1-off ŌåÆ new ledger [[decompiler-atom-log]] (`decompiler-atom-log.md`), one row per atom (shape / forward-lowering / found-in / subs-cleared / ╬ögotos). Walked the 2nd function `init_new_game_state $89A3` (was 16 gotos): derived the target FIRST (an outer redo-`while(1)` wrapping an early-return + 7 for/do-while loops + an if/break), then found ONE atom explained the whole gap. **Atom 3 = routing-block absorption:** a pure-routing `L_X: goto L_Y;` stub (1-succ, no statement ŌĆö the compiler's fall-through forwarder between chained loops, e.g. `$8A05: goto L_8A13`) was BAILED by `_structure_loop`'s adjacency guard on the theory "it emits nothing so the gate can't anchor the exit." **That theory was an untested defensive guess and was WRONG:** the stub emits as an empty block, the gate's `first_real_block` scans PAST it to the real target, and `contract()` drops it on BOTH raw+struct so they match. DELETED the `bounded and routing(e)` clause (+ the now-dead `bounded` param); only the genuine non-adjacent `nxt[max(region)] != e` bail remains; self-validation backstops. **Generalized to 7 subs** (`$89A3` 16ŌåÆ0, `$83E2` 34ŌåÆ30, `$813C`/`$840B`/`$A066` ŌåÆ0, `$90E8`/`$911E` 5ŌåÆ1) ŌĆö a real atom, the `none`-bucket's adjacent-routing slice. **Lesson logged:** audit the other defensive `bounded`/adjacency bails the same way (assume the gate can handle it, test, keep only what self-validation actually rejects). **Still open:** NON-adjacent routing (stub not the address-next block) = the rest of `none` = candidate atom #4. RETURN to the log for the next pick.
>     **Ō¢Č SESSION 9b ŌĆö GUARD AUDIT + ATOM-4 (SWITCH) DEEP-DIVE (2026-06-05, no fold change ŌĆö diagnosis + tooling).** (1) **Guard audit** (`tools/probe-bail-audit.py`, the atom-3 lesson globalized): suppressed every gate-limitation guard via `vm_reduce._AUDIT_SKIP` and measured ŌĆö **atom 3 was the EXCEPTION, not the rule.** 5 of 6 guards are well-calibrated (`arm_order` is load-bearing: +30 gotos if removed); only `merge_not_adjacent` has latent ŌłÆ21 but breaks 5 subs, and routing-skip refinements REGRESSED (routing absorption is LOOP-EXIT-specific, does NOT generalize to if-merges). (2) **Switch deep-dive (atom-4 candidate, [[decompiler-atom-log]]):** switches = **365 gotos across 36 subs, >Ōģō of the 988 corpus** ŌĆö the biggest lever. VM format confirmed (`$D5` contiguous stores `default` BEFORE case targets ŌĆö Chris's "switch{default;case0;ŌĆ”}"; `$D9` noncontiguous default-last; cases fall through C-style). Two failure modes BOTH rooted in the switch's exit `M=post-dom(S)` being a SHARED block (shared returns / pre-switch guards reach it): **(A)** 11 switches fail detection (single-entry / enclosed-domination reject the shared/interleaved M; excluding M recovers only 2/11 ŌĆö multi-shape); **(B)** 8 of 25 detected switches (incl. the corpus's biggest sub `$A2D2`=42 gotos) flat-span in context because the tier-2 post-dom spine cuts AT M while the switch territory straddles it ŌåÆ `cross_edge_top`. **Explored B per Chris's call ŌåÆ "B IS A":** the in-context failure is the same shared/interleaved-merge problem; M is simultaneously the switch exit, a shared block, an interleaved-layout block, AND a spine articulation point ŌĆö all four flavors collapse to "we don't model M as a first-class shared switch-exit." **Ō¢ČŌ¢Č NEXT SESSION (Chris has a plan): the PRINCIPLED atom-4 = model `M=post-dom(S)` as a first-class shared switch EXIT** (excluded from the case-target + enclosed checks; tier-2 must not cut a region inside a switch territory). "An interesting experiment" ŌĆö start from the [[decompiler-atom-log]] atom-4 entry (diagnosis is airtight + won't need re-deriving).
>
> **­¤öÆ DESIGN DECISIONS LOCKED (Chris, 2026-06-04 ŌĆö settled before rung 1, plan-walked against the $E76F corpus):**
>   1. **Rule-match order = a TUNABLE, not a constant.** The fixpoint tries an order (candidate: loop ŌåÆ switch ŌåÆ ifelse ŌåÆ ifthen ŌåÆ short-circuit ŌåÆ seq); a sub that *blocks* (no rule fires where one structurally should) is the signal to permute. Rung-1 harness exposes order as a parameter so it's A/B'd on the corpus, not guessed.
>   2. **Irreducibility is STRUCTURAL; the gate is a pure backstop.** V2 detects "no rule fires ŌåÆ break one edge itself" (rung 6); `structured_equivalent` only catches rule *bugs*, it is NOT the control mechanism (inverts the template era, where gate-reject drove fallback).
>   3. **Re-derive the EMIT; reuse the ANALYSIS.** The detectors are *pure* ŌĆö they nail the simple/base shapes. The reducer's job is to reduce hard shapes DOWN to those base cases by composition, representing nesting with TOKENS (abstract nodes): by the time an outer rule looks, the inner structure is already one token, so every rule sees a clean base case. That IS the closure property from the emit side. So reuse dominators/loops/diamonds/switch detection; build a new region-tree + (addr,indent,text) pretty-printer.
>   4. **Value-diamond / boolean-region PRE-CONTRACTION carries through.** `bytecode_cfg` already contracts these (they're expression-layer, not region-layer); the simple translations the existing code does well survive into V2's CFG unchanged ŌĆö confirm the $E76F interaction at rung 3 (it may make rung 3 *smaller* than planned).
>   - **Canonical new-win exemplar (rung 3):** `$E76F draw_daimyo_portrait` = `if (idx < 53 && daimyo_record[idx+6]) { composite } else { preset } <tail>` ŌĆö short-circuit feeding if/else feeding a seq-tail; templates emit 4 gotos (no composition), V2's grammar nests it.
>
> **Ō£ģ ACCEPTED RESIDUE (closed ŌĆö do NOT reopen as work):** the 7 Phase-3 nested-in-`if`/`while` switches; `$9A0F` fully-rotated loop; every other honest-goto fallback. These were DECISIONS, not TODOs ŌĆö under V2 they re-derive automatically as the irreducible set.
>
> **RULE going forward (the anti-sprawl guard):** a discovery may land in ACCEPTED (honest goto) or the Inbox (a future epic) ŌĆö it may **NOT** add a new OPEN sub-step to this epic. A new open frame is a deliberate decision, never session momentum. Every "DONE" ends with a *return* verdict, not a `Ō¢Č Next`.
>
> ---
> **ŌżĄ SUPERSEDED DETAIL ŌĆö the template-phase history (kept for the record + the fallback structurer; NOT the live frontier; do NOT extend):**
### EPIC (superseded): goto ŌåÆ while / if-else / switch via templates (Chris, 2026-06-03, PROMOTED from "not chased")
> **Why now:** after the teardown (A=table-driven dispatch, C=arg/arity), the *expression* layer of the decompiled C reads like real C ŌĆö the last "assembler smell" is the **1,437 `goto`s + 1,511 `L_XXXX:` labels** (~2,950 lines of scaffolding across 277 of 495 subs; 218 are already goto-free). Folding these into structured `while`/`if-else`/`switch` is the single biggest remaining readability gain. Surfaced concretely by the `vm_bootstrap` two-loop walk (the per-game `init` vs per-turn loop distinction is invisible until the back-edges render as nested `while`).
> **Goto census (measured 2026-06-03, cross-checks the long-standing ~1437 figure):** 451 **backward** (loops) + 986 **forward** (if/break/early-return); 842 conditional `if(..)goto` + 595 bare.
>
> **THE GATE (the crux ŌĆö this epic CANNOT use the byte-identical regen-guard, because structuring deliberately changes the C).** Replacement gate = **CFG-equivalence**: extract the basic-block successor graph from the bytecode (vm-disasm already computes reachability/successors), apply only structuring transforms that **provably lower back to the same CFG**, and **FALL BACK to `goto` on anything unproven** (irreducible regions, overlapping/multi-entry loops). Fidelity then rises monotonically and is *never wrong*. Realistic ceiling is **<100%** ŌĆö even Ghidra/Hex-Rays emit gotos for irreducible control flow; a few honest gotos remaining is CORRECT, not a failure (forcing structure there would lie about the flow). Target ~70ŌĆō90% folded.
> **Not greenfield:** extends the existing `structure_lines` post-pass (already folds `if(!(C))goto;ŌĆ”L:` ŌåÆ `if(C){}` Pattern A + if/else Pattern B). New patterns plug into the same machinery.
>
> **DECISION ŌĆö the artifact is READABLE C, reversibility is a producible WITNESS (Chris, 2026-06-03).** This epic crosses the project's dedeterminism/reversibility line, but precisely: it is NOT non-deterministic (transforms stay pure algorithms in the tool ŌĆö the moment an *agent* eyeballs structure into a hard case, refuse it) and it does NOT touch the M1 byte-identical round-trip (that lives BELOW the C rendering, at bytecodeŌåöstructured-operand ŌĆö `vm_assemble.py` is indifferent to goto-vs-while). What's traded is **text-level losslessness (C line Ōåö instruction) ŌåÆ behavior-level CFG-equivalence.** Chris's call: **structured C (good `if`/`while`/`switch` + brackets) is the ON-BY-DEFAULT canonical file you read**; the raw goto form stays REPRODUCIBLE on demand via `--raw` as the round-trip witness (so the reversible-deterministic artifact is never *lost*, just not the primary surface). Honest inline `goto` stays where the bytecode is genuinely irreducible (correct, not failure ŌĆö Ghidra/Hex-Rays do the same; forcing structure there would lie about the flow). This is the same default-off-switch pattern as `decompile-all.py --self-check` / `all_banks.c`-is-derived, inverted: here the RICHER view is the default and the strict witness is the flag. [[feedback_derived_artifact_is_also_a_deliverable]]
>
> - ­¤¤ó **Phase 0 ŌĆö CFG extractor + raw-witness gate + `--raw` plumbing ŌĆö LANDED 2026-06-03 (hard half done; structured-equivalence RELATION is the open decision before Phase 1).**
>   - **`--raw` plumbing DONE.** `vm_decompile.STRUCTURE` toggle (default True, mirrors the `SELF_CHECK` pattern ŌåÆ canonical `decompiled/*.c` BYTE-IDENTICAL, verified); `decompile-all.py --raw` flips it off ŌåÆ pure goto witness in `decompiled/raw/` (never clobbers canonical, merged view skipped). A `collect=` hook on `decompile()` + `on_sub=` on `bank_subs()` hand the gate each sub's raw+structured line lists + instructions with no risky refactor. All existing gates stay green (round-trip 495/45024, drift-guard 179 gated, full-regen byte-identical).
>   - **CFG extractor + raw lowering DONE & PROVEN (`tools/vm_cfg.py`).** `bytecode_cfg(instructions)` = ground-truth basic-block graph; `lower_goto_cfg(raw, leaders)` lowers the witness to the same graph. **Key key-space insight that makes the gate clean: the decompiler's `L_XXXX` labels ARE bytecode target addresses, so C control flow and bytecode share one coordinate system ŌĆö no name-matching.** Two real bugs found+fixed by going to ground truth (the witness MUST be exact): fall-through has to target the next leader BY ADDRESS, not the next emitted line ŌĆö else (a) the decompiler's out-of-order **flushed-call lines** (a discarded side-effecting CALL is emitted at its flush point but tagged with its earlier addr) and (b) **folded statement-less blocks** (a branch target whose every instr folds into an expression) both mis-route. Per-block address-based lowering is robust to both.
>   - **HARD GATE GREEN (`tools/vm-cfg-gate.py`): `lower_goto_cfg(raw) == bytecode_cfg` 495/495.** Proves `--raw` is a CFG-faithful round-trip witness (the reversibility guarantee, mechanically verified) + the extractor is correct across the whole codebase + no unrecognised control mnemonics.
>   - **ŌÜĀ’ĖÅ THE OPEN DECISION (Chris) ŌĆö the STRUCTURED equivalence RELATION, lock before Phase 1.** Naive `lower(structured) == bytecode_cfg` is the WRONG gate: `structure_lines` already does **destructive folds** that change the block partition while preserving behaviour ŌĆö **early-return** (`if(!C) return X;` merges the separate return-block into the branch block) and **empty-arm if/else** (`if(C){}else{}` collapses a 2-block diamond, stripping the gotos that defined the arms). 263/495 match the strict gate today; the 232 that differ are a MIX of (a) these legit destructive folds and (b) the provisional tree lowering `lower_c_to_cfg` still carrying the same next-leader fall-through bug that `lower_goto_cfg` already fixed (so 232 is an upper bound on "real divergence," not a true count ŌĆö don't read it as 232 bad folds). So Phase 1's gate needs both: fix the structured lowering's fall-through (port the per-block address rule), AND a relation that ACCEPTS valid block-merges but still catches a real misroute. Candidate (designed, not yet built): **contract pure-routing blocks** (goto-only / empty / single-`return V`) on BOTH sides, carrying the **return VALUE on the EXIT edge** (so a wrong/spurious return is caught), PLUS **true/false edge labels** (so a condition inversion in an if/else ŌĆö same nodes, swapped guards ŌĆö is caught; a plain unlabelled CFG would miss it). The provisional tree lowering `lower_c_to_cfg` is the starting point but needs the same next-leader fall-through fix. **Phase 1 opens by locking this relation, then building it + negative-testing it (inject a misroute ŌåÆ must fail).**
>   - ­¤¤ó **STEP 1 DONE 2026-06-03 ŌĆö relation BUILT + it immediately earned its keep (found a real bug).** `vm_cfg.lower_struct_cfg` (correct structured lowering: brace-matched header `(true,false)` edges, address-based merges via the highest LEADER in the span so empty/folded arms resolve, then-tailŌåÆmerge redirect for if-else) + `observable_blocks` + `contract` (bypass pure-routing / bare-`return` blocks) + `structured_equivalent` = `contract(lower_struct) == contract(lower_goto(raw))`. Three real lowering bugs found+fixed en route (then-tail-falls-into-else; merge missed empty-arm leaders; empty-else merge). **Result: hard raw gate 495/495; structured-equivalence 460/495.** **THE 35 RESIDUE IS THE PAYOFF, NOT NOISE:** they're subs where the CURRENT, UNGATED `structure_lines` applied a fold that ISN'T CFG-preserving ŌĆö including a **CONFIRMED CORRECTNESS BUG**: `num_to_ascii` ($CF98, bank 15) structured C nests `L_CFBC:` (the `arg2<arg3` recursive branch) INSIDE the `if(arg2>=arg3){}` braces, so that path falls off the function and returns garbage instead of recursing (raw/bytecode branch to $CFBC; structured goes to EXIT). Others (`$8F14` etc.) are genuinely irreducible (a `goto` jumps INTO the middle of a structured if-body = multi-entry) ŌĆö the EPIC's "leave an honest goto" cases. **So the gate, the moment it existed, proved the pre-EPIC Patterns A/B sometimes emit CFG-WRONG C that's been sitting in `decompiled/*.c`.** Gate is report-mode for the structured check (exit 1 only on the raw witness); the 35 are the Phase-1 work-list.
>   - ~~**Ō¢Č PHASE 1 REFRAME**~~ **DONE 2026-06-03 ŌĆö the 35 are FIXED, gating is wired in.** `vm_decompile.decompile()` now GATES the structuring: after `structure_lines`, it checks `vm_cfg.structured_equivalent(raw, structured, leaders)` and, if the fold is NOT CFG-preserving, reverts that sub to the honest goto form (`collect` exposes `structured_ungated` + `gated_fallback` for the gate tool). **Result: the `num_to_ascii` correctness bug is FIXED** (recursive branch reads correctly again) and all 35 non-CFG-preserving subs revert to goto (`decompiled/*.c` regenerated, net ŌłÆ190 lines; round-trip 495/45024 + drift-guard still CLEAN ŌĆö they're on bytecode, untouched). The gate's structured check is now a **HARD gate**: `vm-cfg-gate.py` = 495/495 witness + **495/495 gated-structuring-is-CFG-preserving** + reports the 35 goto fallbacks. **Non-vacuousness PROVEN** ŌĆö `tools/test-vm-cfg.py` injects a misroute into real subs and asserts the relation REJECTS it (9/9 pass). This is the EPIC's safety mechanism fully operational: **fidelity now rises ONLY where it's provably correct.** Ō¢Č Next: the actual Phase-1 fold (backward goto ŌåÆ `while`/`do-while`), each fold safe-by-construction via this gate. ~~**KNOWN GAP (note for the if-else folder, Phase 2):** the contraction relation catches MISROUTES but not a pure then/else SWAP (same two targets, inverted guard) ŌĆö add true/false EDGE LABELS before Phase 2 leans on it.~~ **CLOSED 2026-06-03 ŌĆö see Phase 2 step 0 below.**
>   - ­¤¤ó **PHASE 1a ŌĆö top-test `while` folds ŌĆö DONE 2026-06-03. 42 loops folded, 84 gotos removed, every gate green, ZERO net new fallbacks.** New CFG substrate in `vm_cfg.py` (`dominators` / `back_edges` / `natural_loop` ŌĆö standard iterative dataflow over the block CFG). New `vm_decompile.structure_loops(lines, instructions)` runs BEFORE `structure_lines` (loops outermost, then if/else folds inside the bodies) and folds a **single-back-edge, single-exit, reducible top-test (`whileTop`) loop** into `while (C) { body }`. CFG-DRIVEN ŌĆö header/body/exit come from the bytecode CFG, never line-text guessing. **The hard case it solves = the ROTATED idiom** (the common compiler shape: test emitted at the BOTTOM, body above, with an entry `goto L_test` guard ŌĆö header address > body address in ~all 60 survey candidates). The fold hoists the test to the top (├Ā la Ghidra/Hex-Rays); to keep `lower_struct_cfg`'s address-based fall-through correct after the hoist, the structured lowering now models a while **position-based** (body-entry/tail/exit = first/last block-occupying line in the braces, NOT `next_leader`) + a **body-leaders entry redirect** (a block before the loop whose address-next leader lands INSIDE the hoisted body enters via the header instead ŌĆö the analogue of the dropped guard goto). **Two real lowering bugs found+fixed en route:** (1) the empty-entry-block case (`$A742`: the guard was the entry block's ONLY statement ŌåÆ dropping it left an empty block that fell through to the body by address) ŌĆö fixed by the body-leaders redirect; (2) `_opens_block` ŌĆö a construct OPENER (`if (C) {` / `while (C) {`) ends in `{` so `_is_scaffold` called it scaffold, but it STARTS a block, so a body beginning with an `if` got the wrong body-entry + a broken redirect (the `for`-style loop `$9E9D`, increment in the header block, was the witness). Fixing it took fallbacks 64 ŌåÆ **35 = the exact pre-loop if/else baseline** (loops add zero new fallbacks; the 5 still-rejected loop-attempts are all subs whose if/else part was already failing). **The decompiled diff is provably a pure structural transform** ŌĆö `git diff -w` shows ONLY `+while` / `+}` / `-goto` / `-L_label` + indentation, ZERO expression/content change. Gates: CFG-gate 495/495 witness + **495/495 gated-structuring-CFG-preserving**, round-trip 495/45024 CLEAN, drift-guard CLEAN, `--check` 0 BAD ├Ś4. **Non-vacuousness for loops PROVEN** ŌĆö `test-vm-cfg.py` (18/18) asserts a folded `while`ŌåÆ`if` (back edge dropped) is REJECTED by the relation. Reads as source now: `avg_daimyo_charisma_over_fief_list` is a clean `while (*p != 255) { ŌĆ” }`; `build_event_eligible_fief_candidate_list` a `while`-with-nested-`if`. **Cosmetic debt (inherited from `structure_lines`, NOT introduced ŌĆö confirmed in the pre-existing committed output): if-bodies aren't extra-indented + occasional dangling merge labels / stray braces; a structure_lines indentation pass would fix it for loops AND ifs at once.**

>     - ­¤¤ó **STEP 2 / sub-problem (c) + a GATE-SOUNDNESS FIX ŌĆö DONE 2026-06-04. The real prize was finding a GATE HOLE.** Added a `while (1)` infinite-loop fold (`_fold_while1`) for switch-header / no-clean-test menu loops: wraps the loop span in `while (1) {}`, the header switch + label stay inside as the loop top, body `goto L_h`ŌåÆ`continue` / `goto L_exit`ŌåÆ`break` (switch CASE gotos keep their labels for Phase 3). Dispatched as a fallback when no 2-way `while`/`do-while` applies. **$AC33 folds** (a clean `while(1){ switch(poll_input()){ŌĆ”} }` combat menu). **But wiring it in surfaced a latent GATE HOLE that had silently accepted 15 WRONG folds:** a loop with a CONDITIONAL back edge `if(C) goto L_h` is a *do-while* (C false = EXIT), but `_fold_while1` rendered it `while(1){ ŌĆ”; if(C) continue; }` ŌĆö making the do-while's exit wrongly LOOP. The gate ACCEPTED it because it modelled a body-tail's fall-through as `next_leader` (the post-loop block), which for a rotated `while(C)` happens to equal the header by address (so it was invisible) but for `while(1)` (tail at the end, header at the top) fabricated a spurious exit edge that matched the bytecode. **Root fix (`vm_cfg.lower_struct_cfg`): a loop body-TAIL's fall goes to the HEADER, not `next_leader`** (`tail_fall_to_header` + `fall_of()`, applied to every fall position ŌĆö ifgoto/ifcontinue/ifbreak/ifreturn/switch-no-default/plain). Proven sound: with the source guard *disabled*, the gate now REJECTS the bad `$830B` fold on its own (reverts to honest goto). **Two-way win:** the corrected model also UNLOCKED 2 valid `while(C)` folds in bank_15 (a strcmp-like `while(*arg1==*arg2)`) the *old buggy model had been false-negative rejecting. Belt-and-suspenders **source guard** in `_fold_while1` too (bail on any 2-way conditional back edge ŌĆö that's do-while territory, not infinite). **Result: 8/9 fold** ($AC33 added); $B6D6/$8C88 correctly DON'T (they have conditional back edges ŌåÆ do-while-with-switch, a deferred shape); $9A0F still the lone messy residue. Loop totals now **81 folded** (70 while + 10 do-while + 1 while1). Gates: cfg-gate 495/495 + 495/495 (35 fallbacks UNCHANGED), round-trip 495/45024 CLEAN, drift CLEAN, `--check` 0 BAD ├Ś4, **test-vm-cfg 54ŌåÆ56** (the new test BUILDS the bad while(1) and asserts the gate REJECTS it ŌĆö the hole-closure proof). Ō¢Č Remaining of the original 9: just $9A0F (messy body) + the $B6D6/$8C88 do-while-with-switch shape (own follow-on). The 68 nested/sibling subs remain the big 4th bucket.

>     - ­¤¤ó **STEP 2 / sub-problem (a) ŌĆö DONE 2026-06-04. Root cause was NOT a merge bug ŌĆö it was a LINE-LESS interior loop block.** `$B1BE` (`submenu_prompt`) folds now.
